# Fix: separate label from data
checks = [
    ("GHA-PAN Q8 Ghana 3+SOT", 0.45, 0.66),
    ("GHA-PAN Q2 Panama offsides", 0.28, 0.44),
    ("ENG-CRO Q6 England more fouls", 0.15, 0.43),
    ("ENG-CRO Q2 Croatia offsides", 0.26, 0.45),
    ("GHA-PAN Q5 Ghana more 2H SOT", 0.40, 0.54),
    ("UZB-COL Q2 COL more 2H SOT", 0.62, 0.69),
]

print("=== CROWD FORMULA VALIDATION (crowd ~= 0.514 + 0.61*(us-0.5)) ===")
residuals = []
for label, us, crowd_actual in checks:
    pred = 0.514 + 0.61*(us-0.5)
    diff = crowd_actual - pred
    residuals.append(diff)
    print(f"  {label}:")
    print(f"    us={us}, pred_crowd={pred:.3f}, actual_crowd={crowd_actual}, residual={diff:+.3f}")

print(f"\n  Mean residual: {sum(residuals)/len(residuals):+.3f}pp (positive = crowd MORE bullish than formula predicts)")
print(f"  All 6 residuals positive: crowd systematically ABOVE formula in this batch")

print("\n=== OFFSIDES FAMILY COMPLETE RECORD ===")
# From memory: 5/5 before BEL-EGY; BEL-EGY was 6th; then presumably more
# From context: "now 9/9 NO" was mentioned in the prior session output
offsides_record = [
    ("BRA-MAR",     0.35, 0.47, 0, "+20.36"),
    ("GER-CUR",     0.43, 0.54, 0, "+13.79"),
    ("JPN-NED",     0.36, 0.49, 0, "+12.02"),
    ("CIV-ECU",     0.22, 0.31, 0, "+9.97"),
    ("BEL-EGY",     0.54, 0.64, 0, "-1.57"),  # first >0.5, still NO
    ("SAU-URU",     "n/a","n/a", "n/a", "n/a"),  # not sure if this had one
    ("GHA-PAN Q2",  0.28, 0.44, 0, "+13.60"),
    ("ENG-CRO Q2",  0.26, 0.45, 0, "+15.73"),
    ("UZB-COL Q1",  0.45, 0.42, 0, "0.00"),
]
print(f"  Match count with offsides: {len([x for x in offsides_record if x[3]!='n/a'])}")
print(f"  All resolved NO (0 outcomes). Running total from this prop type: massive positive.")
print(f"  GHA-PAN: Panama had 1 offside. ENG-CRO: Croatia had 1 offside. UZB-COL: Uzbekistan had 0 offsides.")

print("\n=== SUBMISSION ERROR IMPACT (ENG-CRO Q7 Kane 2H SOT) ===")
submitted = 0.20
recommended = 0.43
crowd = 0.59
outcome = 1.0
rbp_submitted = -44.55
# Estimate loss at 0.43
sq_err_sub = (outcome - submitted)**2
sq_err_rec = (outcome - recommended)**2
sq_err_crowd = (outcome - crowd)**2
# RBP = k*(crowd_sq_err - our_sq_err) per question, k varies
# Use actual RBP to back out k
k = abs(rbp_submitted) / (sq_err_sub - sq_err_crowd)
rbp_rec = k * (sq_err_crowd - sq_err_rec)
print(f"  Submitted: {submitted}, Sq err: {sq_err_sub:.4f}")
print(f"  Recommended: {recommended}, Sq err: {sq_err_rec:.4f}")
print(f"  Crowd: {crowd}, Sq err: {sq_err_crowd:.4f}")
print(f"  Actual RBP at submission (0.20): {rbp_submitted}")
print(f"  Implied question scale k: {k:.2f}")
print(f"  Estimated RBP at recommended (0.43): {rbp_rec:+.1f}")
print(f"  Error cost (extra RBP lost): {rbp_submitted - rbp_rec:+.1f}")

print("\n=== LOSING TEAM PLAYER PROP PATTERN ===")
print("  Fajardo (Panama lost 0-1 to Ghana):")
print("    us=0.57 (market), crowd=0.39, outcome=0 (0 SOT), RBP=-13.82")
print("    Panama total: 4 SOT, 11 shots. Fajardo=0 SOT despite team having shots.")
print("  Sucic (Croatia lost 4-2 to England):")
print("    us=0.43 (market), crowd=0.34, outcome=0 (0 SOT), RBP=-3.45")
print("  Both: crowd CORRECTLY priced losing team's forward BELOW our market estimate.")
print("  Pattern: market prices attacker SOT pre-match at 'typical output'.")
print("           But in a losing team, the manager adjusts tactically (sit back/defensive),")
print("           limiting attacking opportunities for individual forwards.")
print("  NEW RULE 15 CANDIDATE: for player SOT/goal props, shade losing-team forwards")
print("  DOWN from market price by ~10-15pp when team is expected to lose OR is trailing.")

print("\n=== RUNNING TOTALS ===")
prior = 189.18
batch = 67.91 + 39.45 + 1.16
new_total = prior + batch
print(f"  Prior total: +{prior}")
print(f"  This batch (3 matches, 30 questions): +{batch:.2f}")
print(f"  New running total: +{new_total:.2f}")
print(f"  Match count: ~14 total")
print(f"  Questions count: ~125 total (prior ~105 + 30 new)")
print(f"  Hypothetical total (correct Kane submission): +{new_total + 44.55 - 15:.2f}")

import json

### CMD #7
# DESC: Run worked math examples for all four key questions
# ID: toolu_0127zSsMKB6bYV8gsHjgTX6T
```
python3 << 'EOF'
import json, math
from scipy.stats import poisson, skellam

# ========== WORKED EXAMPLE: Ghana 3+ SOT (Q8) ==========
print("=" * 60)
print("WORKED EXAMPLE 1: Ghana 3+ SOT (Q8) — Poisson")
print("=" * 60)

# Ghana's recent SOT data (n=4 matches from ESPN)
ghana_sot = [1, 1, 3, 5]   # Austria(A), Germany(A), Mexico(H), Wales(A)
lam = sum(ghana_sot) / len(ghana_sot)   # = 2.5
print(f"  Ghana SOT per match: {ghana_sot}")
print(f"  Lambda (sample mean): {lam}")

# Poisson P(X >= 3) = 1 - P(X=0) - P(X=1) - P(X=2)
p0 = math.exp(-lam)               # P(X=0)
p1 = math.exp(-lam) * lam         # P(X=1)
p2 = math.exp(-lam) * lam**2 / 2  # P(X=2)
p_at_least_3 = 1 - p0 - p1 - p2
print(f"\n  P(X=0) = e^-{lam} = {p0:.4f}")
print(f"  P(X=1) = e^-{lam} × {lam} = {p1:.4f}")
print(f"  P(X=2) = e^-{lam} × {lam}^2 / 2 = {p2:.4f}")
print(f"  P(X≥3) = 1 - {p0:.4f} - {p1:.4f} - {p2:.4f} = {p_at_least_3:.4f}")
print(f"\n  → Our estimate: 0.45 (lightly shaded from {p_at_least_3:.3f})")
print(f"  → Crowd estimate: 0.66")
print(f"  → Actual: Ghana had 2 SOT (outcome = NO)")
print(f"  → RBP gain: +25.72")

print()
print("=" * 60)
print("WORKED EXAMPLE 2: Panama 2+ offsides (Q10) — Poisson + RULE12")
print("=" * 60)

panama_offsides = [5, 0, 1]  # South Africa, South Africa, Brazil
lam_raw = sum(panama_offsides) / len(panama_offsides)  # = 2.0
lam_deoutliered = sum([0, 1]) / 2   # remove 5-offside outlier

p_raw = 1 - math.exp(-lam_raw) * (1 + lam_raw)
p_deoutliered = 1 - math.exp(-lam_deoutliered) * (1 + lam_deoutliered)

print(f"  Panama offsides per match: {panama_offsides}")
print(f"  Lambda (raw mean): {lam_raw}")
print(f"  P(X≥2) raw = 1 - e^-{lam_raw}×(1+{lam_raw}) = {p_raw:.3f}")
print(f"\n  Outlier check: 5 offsides vs South Africa dominates the average")
print(f"  Lambda (de-outlied): {lam_deoutliered}")
print(f"  P(X≥2) de-outlied = {p_deoutliered:.3f}")
print(f"  Sensitivity: {abs(p_raw - p_deoutliered):.3f} — massive RULE12 trigger")
print(f"\n  Decision: shade heavily toward de-outlied estimate")
print(f"  → Our estimate: 0.28  (between 0.09 and 0.594, near the low end)")
print(f"  → Crowd estimate: 0.44")
print(f"  → Actual: Panama had 1 offside (outcome = NO)")
print(f"  → RBP gain: +13.60")

print()
print("=" * 60)
print("WORKED EXAMPLE 3: Ghana more 2H SOT than Panama (Q1) — Skellam")
print("=" * 60)

# Skellam: difference of two independent Poissons
# Ghana 2H lambda = avg_SOT_full / 2 = 2.5 / 2 = 1.25
# Panama 2H lambda = avg_SOT_full (de-outlied) / 2 = 3.0 / 2 = 1.5
lam_g = 2.5 / 2
lam_p_full = 3.0 / 2   # de-outlied (without 9-SOT Brazil game)
lam_p_raw = 5.0 / 2    # raw (including outlier)

# P(Ghana > Panama) = P(X_G - X_P > 0) where X_G - X_P ~ Skellam(lam_g, lam_p)
# Skellam mean = lam_g - lam_p = 1.25 - 1.5 = -0.25  (slightly Panama-favored)
p_g_more_deoutliered = skellam.sf(0, lam_g, lam_p_full)  # P(D > 0)
p_g_more_raw = skellam.sf(0, lam_g, lam_p_raw)

print(f"  Ghana 2H lambda (avg SOT 2.5, half): {lam_g}")
print(f"  Panama 2H lambda (de-outlied avg 3.0, half): {lam_p_full}")
print(f"  Panama 2H lambda (raw avg 5.0, half): {lam_p_raw}")
print(f"  Skellam mean = {lam_g} - {lam_p_full} = {lam_g - lam_p_full:.2f}")
print(f"  P(Ghana > Panama, de-outlied) = {p_g_more_deoutliered:.3f}")
print(f"  P(Ghana > Panama, raw) = {p_g_more_raw:.3f}")
print(f"  Sensitivity: {abs(p_g_more_deoutliered - p_g_more_raw):.3f}")
print(f"\n  Decision: settle between raw (0.26) and de-outlied (0.44)")
print(f"  Corner market is 50/50, draw price 30.2% (RULE8 max)")
print(f"  → Our estimate: 0.40")
print(f"  → Crowd estimate: 0.54")
print(f"  → Actual: Panama had MORE SOT (outcome = NO)")
print(f"  → RBP gain: +16.21")

print()
print("=" * 60)
print("WORKED EXAMPLE 4: Kane 2H SOT (ENG-CRO Q5) — market-derived Poisson")
print("=" * 60)

kane_full_market = 0.6734   # Smarkets mid price
# Model Kane's SOT as Poisson: P(1+ in full match) = 1 - e^-lambda
# → lambda = -ln(1 - 0.6734)
lam_kane_full = -math.log(1 - kane_full_market)
lam_kane_2h = lam_kane_full / 2
p_kane_2h = 1 - math.exp(-lam_kane_2h)
print(f"  Smarkets full-match Kane SOT market: {kane_full_market}")
print(f"  Convert to Poisson lambda: lambda = -ln(1-{kane_full_market}) = {lam_kane_full:.4f}")
print(f"  2H lambda = {lam_kane_full:.4f} / 2 = {lam_kane_2h:.4f}")
print(f"  P(Kane 1+ SOT in 2H) = 1 - e^-{lam_kane_2h:.4f} = {p_kane_2h:.4f}")
print(f"\n  → RECOMMENDED estimate: 0.43")
print(f"  → SUBMITTED estimate: 0.20 (SUBMISSION ERROR)")
print(f"  → Crowd estimate: 0.59")
print(f"  → Actual: Kane had 1+ SOT in 2H (outcome = YES)")

sq_err_submitted = (1 - 0.20)**2
sq_err_recommended = (1 - 0.43)**2
sq_err_crowd = (1 - 0.59)**2
print(f"\n  Squared errors:")
print(f"    Submitted 0.20: (1-0.20)² = {sq_err_submitted:.4f}")
print(f"    Recommended 0.43: (1-0.43)² = {sq_err_recommended:.4f}")
print(f"    Crowd 0.59: (1-0.59)² = {sq_err_crowd:.4f}")
print(f"  RBP formula (conceptually): k × (crowd_sq_err - our_sq_err)")
print(f"    At 0.20: k × ({sq_err_crowd:.4f} - {sq_err_submitted:.4f}) = k × {sq_err_crowd - sq_err_submitted:.4f} → -44.55")
print(f"    At 0.43: k × ({sq_err_crowd:.4f} - {sq_err_recommended:.4f}) = k × {sq_err_crowd - sq_err_recommended:.4f} → ~-14.8")
EOF

```

  P(X=1) = e^-2.5 × 2.5 = 0.2052
  P(X=2) = e^-2.5 × 2.5^2 / 2 = 0.2565
  P(X≥3) = 1 - 0.0821 - 0.2052 - 0.2565 = 0.4562

  → Our estimate: 0.45 (lightly shaded from 0.456)
  → Crowd estimate: 0.66

  Lambda (de-outlied): 0.5

  Sensitivity: 0.504 — massive RULE12 trigger

  → Actual: Panama had 1 offside (outcome = NO)
  → RBP gain: +13.60

  Panama 2H lambda (de-outlied avg 3.0, half): 1.5
  Panama 2H lambda (raw avg 5.0, half): 2.5
  Skellam mean = 1.25 - 1.5 = -0.25
  P(Ghana > Panama, de-outlied) = 0.316
  P(Ghana > Panama, raw) = 0.175
  Sensitivity: 0.142

### CMD #11
# DESC: Pull both teams' WC2026 group stage boxscores
# ID: toolu_01LJMabzXLMMin5LQRUQWXZp
```
# Pull Switzerland's WC match vs Qatar (event 760420 from qat_sui file)
# and Bosnia's WC match vs Canada (event 760416 from can_bih file)
python3 << 'EOF'
import json, urllib.request

def get_match(eid, label):
    url = f"https://site.api.espn.com/apis/site/v2/sports/soccer/fifa.world/summary?event={eid}"
    with urllib.request.urlopen(url) as r:
        d = json.loads(r.read())
    print(f"\n{'='*20} {label} (event {eid}) {'='*20}")
    for team in d['boxscore']['teams']:
        stats = {s['name']: s.get('displayValue') for s in team['statistics']}
        print(f"  {team['team']['displayName']}: fouls={stats.get('foulsCommitted')} YC={stats.get('yellowCards')} RC={stats.get('redCards')} offsides={stats.get('offsides')} SOT={stats.get('shotsOnTarget')} shots={stats.get('totalShots')} corners={stats.get('cornerKicks')} poss={stats.get('possessionPct')}")
    for ev in d.get('keyEvents',[]):
        typ = ev.get('type',{}).get('text','')
        if any(x in typ for x in ['Goal','Card']):
            print(f"    {ev.get('clock',{}).get('displayValue','?')}' | {typ} | {ev.get('team',{}).get('displayName','')} | {ev.get('text','')[:80]}")

# QAT-SUI: Switzerland vs Qatar
get_match(760420, "QAT-SUI (Switzerland's WC match 1)")
# CAN-BIH: Bosnia vs Canada
get_match(760416, "CAN-BIH (Bosnia's WC match 1)")
EOF
```

### CMD #20
# DESC: Pull actual Smarkets bid/offer quotes for SUI-BIH markets
# ID: toolu_01FHhtwnVAwiEBcUtdvKQHCi
```
# Pull actual quotes (bid/offer) from Smarkets
python3 << 'PYEOF'
import subprocess, json

def get_mid(mid):
    r = subprocess.run(['curl','-sk',f'https://api.smarkets.com/v3/markets/{mid}/quotes/'],
                       capture_output=True, text=True)
    try:
        return json.loads(r.stdout)
    except:
        return {}

# Key markets
market_ids = {
    "137949816": "Full-time result",
    "137949853": "Over/under 2.5",
    "137949852": "Over/under 1.5",
    "137949846": "BTTS + over 2.5",
    "137949818": "BTTS",
    "137949887": "Asian HCP SUI -2.5",
    "137949899": "Asian HCP SUI -0.5",
    "137949902": "Asian HCP BIH -0.5",
    "145290456": "Player SOT >0.5",
}

for mid, name in market_ids.items():
    d = get_mid(mid)
    quotes = d.get('quotes', {})
    print(f"\n{name} (market {mid}):")
    for contract_id, cq in quotes.items():
        bids = cq.get('bids', [])
        offers = cq.get('offers', [])
        best_bid = bids[0][0]/10000 if bids else None
        best_offer = offers[0][0]/10000 if offers else None
        mid_price = (best_bid + best_offer)/2 if best_bid and best_offer else (best_offer or best_bid)
        print(f"  contract {contract_id}: bid={best_bid} offer={best_offer} mid={mid_price:.4f}" if mid_price else f"  contract {contract_id}: no quotes")
PYEOF
```

### OUT

Over/under 2.5 (market 137949853):

Over/under 1.5 (market 137949852):

BTTS + over 2.5 (market 137949846):

Asian HCP SUI -2.5 (market 137949887):

Asian HCP SUI -0.5 (market 137949899):

### CMD #22
# DESC: Get contract IDs then batch-fetch quotes from Smarkets
# ID: toolu_01MHSttCVsK4ZvfmLKteod7e
```
python3 << 'PYEOF'
import subprocess, json

def api(path):
    r = subprocess.run(['curl','-sk', f'https://api.smarkets.com/v3/{path}'], capture_output=True, text=True)
    try:
        return json.loads(r.stdout)
    except:
        return {}

# Get contracts with IDs first
key_markets = {
    "137949816": "Full-time result",
    "137949853": "Over/under 2.5",
    "137949852": "Over/under 1.5",
    "137949846": "BTTS + over 2.5",
    "137949818": "BTTS",
    "137949851": "Over/under 0.5",
    "137949899": "Asian HCP SUI -0.5",
}

contract_map = {}  # contract_id -> (name, market_name)

for mid, mname in key_markets.items():
    d = api(f'markets/{mid}/contracts/')
    for c in d.get('contracts', []):
        cid = c['id']
        cname = c['name']
        contract_map[cid] = (cname, mname, mid)
    print(f"{mname}: {[c['name']+':'+str(c['id']) for c in d.get('contracts',[])]}")

# Now get all quotes in one batch (Smarkets allows multi-market quote fetch)
market_ids = ','.join(key_markets.keys())
q = api(f'markets/quotes/?market_ids={market_ids}')
print(f"\nQuotes response keys: {list(q.keys())}")
print(f"Sample: {json.dumps(q)[:500]}")
PYEOF
```

### OUT

### CMD #23
# DESC: Fetch Smarkets quotes using contract IDs
# ID: toolu_01P9D5ga4Z1935ZTvLyqTzMu
```
python3 << 'PYEOF'
import subprocess, json

def api(path):
    r = subprocess.run(['curl','-sk', f'https://api.smarkets.com/v3/{path}'], capture_output=True, text=True)
    try:
        return json.loads(r.stdout)
    except:
        return {}

# Use the correct Smarkets quote endpoint format
contract_batches = {
    "FTR": ["387268869","387268871","387268870"],
    "O/U 2.5": ["387269033","387269034"],
    "O/U 1.5": ["387269031","387269032"],
    "O/U 0.5": ["387269029","387269030"],
    "BTTS": ["387268891","387268892"],
    "BTTS+O2.5": ["387269005","387269006","387269007","387269008"],
    "AH SUI -0.5": ["387269125","387269126"],
}

contract_names = {
    "387268869": "Switzerland(W)", "387268871": "Draw", "387268870": "BIH(W)",
    "387269033": "Under 2.5", "387269034": "Over 2.5",
    "387269031": "Under 1.5", "387269032": "Over 1.5",
    "387269029": "Under 0.5", "387269030": "Over 0.5",
    "387268891": "BTTS Yes", "387268892": "BTTS No",
    "387269005": "BTTS+O Yes/Over", "387269006": "BTTS+O Yes/Under",
    "387269007": "BTTS+O No/Over", "387269008": "BTTS+O No/Under",
    "387269125": "SUI -0.5", "387269126": "BIH +0.5",
}

for batch_name, cids in contract_batches.items():
    ids_str = ','.join(cids)
    d = api(f'contracts/quotes/?contract_ids={ids_str}')
    quotes = d.get('quotes', {})
    print(f"\n{batch_name}:")
    for cid in cids:
        cname = contract_names.get(cid, cid)
        cq = quotes.get(cid, {})
        bids = cq.get('bids', [])
        offers = cq.get('offers', [])
        best_bid = bids[0][0]/10000 if bids else None
        best_offer = offers[0][0]/10000 if offers else None
        mid = (best_bid + best_offer)/2 if best_bid and best_offer else (best_offer or best_bid)
        if mid:
            vig_note = ""
            print(f"  {cname}: bid={best_bid:.4f} offer={best_offer:.4f} mid={mid:.4f}")
        else:
            print(f"  {cname}: no quotes yet")
PYEOF

### CMD #27
# DESC: Run full Poisson/Skellam pricing model for SUI-BIH
# ID: toolu_015VMvD97GKhkvVRFXXD8jiQ
```
python3 << 'EOF'
import math
from scipy.stats import poisson, skellam

print("=" * 65)
print("SUI vs BIH — COMPLETE PRICING MODEL")
print("=" * 65)

# ============================================================
# DATA INPUTS
# ============================================================
# Switzerland (n=9 recent: 8 pre-WC + WC vs Qatar)
sui_fouls =   [10,10,8,6,9,13,5,10,11]   # avg pre-WC=8.875, WC=11, n=9 avg=9.11
sui_offsides= [4,3,1,0,1,0,2,1,1]         # n=9, avg=1.44
sui_sot =     [3,10,1,3,3,7,3,8,7]        # n=9, avg=5.0
sui_corners = [None]*8 + [None]            # no corner data from ESPN

# Bosnia (n=6: 5 WCQ ESPN + WC vs Canada)
bih_fouls =   [18,20,9,15,19,20]          # WCQ avg=16.2 (n=5), WC=20, n=6 avg=17.0
bih_sot =     [11,5,1,4,6,3]              # n=6, avg=5.0
bih_offsides= [0,0,0,0,0,0]              # CONFIRMED: 0 in every match! n=6

# Tournament context
sui_fouls_tournament = [12,17,14,10,13,11,14,9,13]  # WC2022+Euro2024, n=9, avg=12.56
sui_offsides_tournament = [2,1,0,3,2,5,2,0,0]       # n=9, avg=1.67

# Lambda calculations
lam_sui_fouls = sum(sui_fouls)/len(sui_fouls)
lam_sui_offsides = sum(sui_offsides)/len(sui_offsides)
lam_sui_sot = sum(sui_sot)/len(sui_sot)
lam_bih_fouls = sum(bih_fouls)/len(bih_fouls)
lam_bih_sot = sum(bih_sot)/len(bih_sot)
lam_bih_offsides = sum(bih_offsides)/len(bih_offsides)
lam_sui_fouls_tournament = sum(sui_fouls_tournament)/len(sui_fouls_tournament)

print(f"\n  Switzerland lambdas (n=9 inc WC): fouls={lam_sui_fouls:.2f}, offsides={lam_sui_offsides:.2f}, SOT={lam_sui_sot:.2f}")
print(f"  Switzerland tournament fouls (n=9): lambda={lam_sui_fouls_tournament:.2f}")
print(f"  Bosnia lambdas (n=6 inc WC): fouls={lam_bih_fouls:.2f}, offsides={lam_bih_offsides:.2f}, SOT={lam_bih_sot:.2f}")
print(f"  Bosnia offsides: {bih_offsides} → ALL ZEROS!")

# ============================================================
# Q: WILL BOSNIA COMMIT MORE FOULS THAN SWITZERLAND?
# ============================================================
print("\n" + "="*65)
print("Q: BOSNIA more fouls than SWITZERLAND (Skellam)")
print("="*65)

# Apples-to-apples: WC context
# SUI tournament: 12.56 (n=9), WC2026 vs Qatar: 11 → use 12.0 blended
# BIH WC: 20 (n=1), WCQ: 16.2 (n=5), n=6 avg: 17.0
lam_sui_f = 12.0   # tournament context
lam_bih_f = 17.0   # tournament context blended
p_bih_more_fouls = skellam.sf(0, lam_bih_f, lam_sui_f)
p_tie_fouls = skellam.pmf(0, lam_bih_f, lam_sui_f)
print(f"  λ_BIH={lam_bih_f} (n=6 WC context), λ_SUI={lam_sui_f} (tournament context)")
print(f"  Skellam P(BIH > SUI fouls) = {p_bih_more_fouls:.4f}")
print(f"  Skellam P(TIE) = {p_tie_fouls:.4f}")
print(f"  RULE12 check: BIH raw={lam_bih_fouls:.1f}, de-outlied (excl 20-foul WC game)={16.2:.1f}")
print(f"  De-outlied Skellam: P(BIH>SUI at 16.2 vs 12.0)={skellam.sf(0, 16.2, 12.0):.4f}")
print(f"  Outlier sensitivity: {abs(p_bih_more_fouls - skellam.sf(0,16.2,12.0)):.4f} → STABLE direction")
print(f"  *** RECOMMENDED: ~{p_bih_more_fouls:.2f} (HIGH CONFIDENCE, signal robust ***)")

# ============================================================
# Q: WILL SWITZERLAND BE CAUGHT OFFSIDE 2+ TIMES?
# ============================================================
print("\n" + "="*65)
print("Q: SWITZERLAND 2+ offsides (Poisson)")
print("="*65)
lam_sui_off = sum(sui_offsides)/len(sui_offsides)  # 1.44
p_sui_2plus_off = 1 - math.exp(-lam_sui_off)*(1 + lam_sui_off)
print(f"  λ_SUI={lam_sui_off:.2f} (n=9 avg: {sui_offsides})")
print(f"  P(X≥2) = 1 - e^-{lam_sui_off:.2f}*(1+{lam_sui_off:.2f}) = {p_sui_2plus_off:.4f}")
lam_suit = 1.67
p_suit = 1 - math.exp(-lam_suit)*(1 + lam_suit)
print(f"  Tournament lambda=1.67: P(X≥2)={p_suit:.4f}")
lam_blend = (lam_sui_off + lam_suit)/2
p_blend = 1 - math.exp(-lam_blend)*(1 + lam_blend)
print(f"  Blended lambda={lam_blend:.2f}: P(X≥2)={p_blend:.4f}")
print(f"  FAMILY CONTEXT: 2+ offsides is 9/9 NO in our history. BUT this is for SUI (attacking team).")
print(f"  Bosnia's deep block may actually CREATE more offsides (same Qatar finding last match!)")
print(f"  *** RECOMMENDED: ~0.40-0.42 (true-probability, no family-pattern shade since SUI=attacker) ***")

# ============================================================
# Q: WILL BOSNIA BE CAUGHT OFFSIDE 2+ TIMES?
# ============================================================
print("\n" + "="*65)
print("Q: BOSNIA 2+ offsides (Poisson)")
print("="*65)
print(f"  Bosnia offsides all matches: {bih_offsides} → λ=0.00")
print(f"  P(X≥2) at λ=0 = 0.000")
print(f"  HOWEVER: n=6 with ALL zeros = extreme. True rate likely 0.2-0.4 due to sample limitation.")
print(f"  Bosnia is a defensive team that rarely pushes high line → physically very low offside rate")
print(f"  Estimate λ=0.2-0.3 (floor): P(X≥2) = {1-math.exp(-0.25)*(1+0.25):.4f}")
print(f"  *** RECOMMENDED: ~0.03-0.05 (extremely low) ***")

# ============================================================
# Q: SWITZERLAND 3+ SOT or 4+ SOT
# ============================================================
print("\n" + "="*65)
print("Q: SWITZERLAND N+ shots on target")
print("="*65)
lam_sui_s = lam_sui_sot  # 5.0
for thresh in [3, 4, 5, 6]:
    p = sum(poisson.pmf(k, lam_sui_s) for k in range(thresh, 20))
    print(f"  P(SUI SOT ≥ {thresh}) = {p:.4f}  [λ={lam_sui_s}]")
print(f"\n  Context: SUI had 7 SOT vs Qatar despite low-block. Strong attacking team.")
print(f"  Against Bosnia (also low-block), expect similar or more SOT.")
print(f"  *** RECOMMENDED for 3+: ~0.77, for 4+: ~0.67, for 5+: ~0.56 ***")

# ============================================================
# Q: WILL BOTH TEAMS SCORE AND MATCH HAVE 3+ GOALS (BTTS+Over2.5)
# ============================================================
print("\n" + "="*65)

python3 << 'PYEOF'
import subprocess, json

# Try v3/markets with all IDs at once - maybe these have prices embedded
key_ids = ["137949862","137949871","137949881","137949841","137949816","137949853"]
for mid in key_ids:
    r = subprocess.run(['curl','-sk', f'https://api.smarkets.com/v3/markets/{mid}/'],
                       capture_output=True, text=True)
    try:
        d = json.loads(r.stdout)
        m = d.get('market', d)
        print(f"{m.get('name', mid)}: state={m.get('state')} | {list(m.keys())[:6]}")
    except:
        pass

# Try fetching from a different endpoint format
print("\n--- Trying event-level markets with embedded prices ---")
r = subprocess.run(['curl','-sk', 'https://api.smarkets.com/v3/events/45042834/markets/?with_contracts=true'],
                   capture_output=True, text=True)
d = json.loads(r.stdout)
for m in d.get('markets', [])[:5]:
    print(f"  {m['name']}: {list(m.keys())}")

python3 << 'PYEOF'
import subprocess, json

# Fetch FTR + goal total contracts
contract_ids = [
    "387268869",  # SUI win
    "387268871",  # Draw
    "387268870",  # BIH win
    "387269033",  # U 2.5
    "387269034",  # O 2.5
    "387269031",  # U 1.5
    "387269032",  # O 1.5
    "387268891",  # BTTS Yes
    "387268892",  # BTTS No
    "387269005",  # BTTS+O2.5 Yes
]
ids_str = ",".join(contract_ids)
r = subprocess.run(['curl','-sk',
    f'https://api.smarkets.com/v3/contracts/quotes/?contract_ids={ids_str}'],
    capture_output=True, text=True)
d = json.loads(r.stdout)
quotes = d.get('quotes', {})
print(f"Got {len(quotes)} quote entries")
for cid, q in quotes.items():
    bid = q.get('bids', [{}])[0].get('price', 'N/A') if q.get('bids') else 'N/A'
    offer = q.get('offers', [{}])[0].get('price', 'N/A') if q.get('offers') else 'N/A'
    print(f"  {cid}: bid={bid} offer={offer}")
print("---")
print("Raw response:", r.stdout[:500] if not quotes else "(quotes populated)")

import subprocess, json

# Get all contracts from FTR and goal markets, then try the quotes endpoint  
market_ids = ["137949816", "137949853", "137949852", "137949818", "137949846",
              "137949841", "137949862", "137949871", "137949881", "137949970"]

all_contracts = {}
for mid in market_ids:
    r = subprocess.run(['curl','-sk', f'https://api.smarkets.com/v3/markets/{mid}/contracts/'],
                       capture_output=True, text=True)
    d = json.loads(r.stdout)
    for c in d.get('contracts', []):
        all_contracts[c['id']] = c['name']

print(f"Total contracts: {len(all_contracts)}")
for cid, name in all_contracts.items():
    print(f"  {cid}: {name}")

# Now try to get quotes
ids_str = ",".join(list(all_contracts.keys()))
print(f"\nFetching quotes...")
r2 = subprocess.run(['curl','-sk',
    f'https://api.smarkets.com/v3/contracts/quotes/?contract_ids={ids_str}'],
    capture_output=True, text=True)
d2 = json.loads(r2.stdout)
quotes = d2.get('quotes', {})
print(f"Quotes count: {len(quotes)}")
if not quotes:
    print("Raw:", r2.stdout[:300])
for cid, q in quotes.items():
    bid = q.get('bids', [{}])[0].get('price') if q.get('bids') else None
    offer = q.get('offers', [{}])[0].get('price') if q.get('offers') else None
    print(f"  {all_contracts.get(cid, cid)}: bid={bid} offer={offer}")

### CMD #38
# DESC: Fetch all key SUI-BIH Smarkets quotes using correct endpoint
# ID: toolu_0142b5JDi9ffMkWnYjtCR48j
```
python3 << 'PYEOF'
import subprocess, json, math

# Define market IDs and their contracts from what we gathered
market_info = {
    "137949816": {"name":"FTR", "contracts":{"387268869":"SUI","387268871":"Draw","387268870":"BIH"}},
    "137949853": {"name":"OU2.5", "contracts":{"387269033":"Under2.5","387269034":"Over2.5"}},
    "137949852": {"name":"OU1.5", "contracts":{"387269031":"Under1.5","387269032":"Over1.5"}},
    "137949818": {"name":"BTTS",  "contracts":{"387268891":"BTTS_Yes","387268892":"BTTS_No"}},
    "137949846": {"name":"BTTS+OU2.5", "contracts":{"387269005":"Yes_Over","387269006":"Yes_Under",
                                                     "387269007":"No_Over","387269008":"No_Under"}},
    "137949841": {"name":"Penalty", "contracts":{"387268979":"Pen_Yes","387268980":"Pen_No"}},
    "137949862": {"name":"2H_OU1.5", "contracts":{"387269051":"2H_Under1.5","387269052":"2H_Over1.5"}},
    "137949871": {"name":"2H_SUI_OU0.5", "contracts":{"387269069":"SUI_2H_Under0.5","387269070":"SUI_2H_Over0.5"}},
    "137949881": {"name":"2H_BIH_OU0.5", "contracts":{"387269089":"BIH_2H_Under0.5","387269090":"BIH_2H_Over0.5"}},
    "137949970": {"name":"Cards_OU2.5", "contracts":{"387269295":"Cards_Under2.5","387269296":"Cards_Over2.5"}},
}

results = {}
for mid, info in market_info.items():
    r = subprocess.run(['curl','-sk', f'https://api.smarkets.com/v3/markets/{mid}/quotes/'],
                       capture_output=True, text=True)
    try:
        quotes = json.loads(r.stdout)
        mid_results = {}
        for cid, cname in info['contracts'].items():
            q = quotes.get(cid, {})
            bid_price = q.get('bids', [{}])[0].get('price') if q.get('bids') else None
            offer_price = q.get('offers', [{}])[0].get('price') if q.get('offers') else None
            # Smarkets prices are in % * 100 (i.e., 6250 = 62.50%)
            bid_pct = bid_price/10000 if bid_price else None
            offer_pct = offer_price/10000 if offer_price else None
            mid_price = (bid_pct + offer_pct)/2 if bid_pct and offer_pct else (bid_pct or offer_pct)
            mid_results[cname] = {"bid": bid_pct, "offer": offer_pct, "mid": mid_price}
        results[info['name']] = mid_results
        print(f"\n{info['name']}:")
        for cn, v in mid_results.items():
            print(f"  {cn}: bid={v['bid']:.4f} offer={v['offer']:.4f} mid={v['mid']:.4f}" if v['mid'] else f"  {cn}: NO QUOTES")
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"Error for {mid}: {e}")

print("\n\n=== SAVING RAW RESULTS ===")
with open('/Users/aki/Desktop/QK Rstudio/sportspredict_research/data/external_markets/sui_bih_smarkets_quotes.json', 'w') as f:
    json.dump(results, f, indent=2)
print("Saved to sui_bih_smarkets_quotes.json")
PYEOF
```

### CMD #39
# DESC: Run full pricing model with live market data and ESPN Poisson/Skellam
# ID: toolu_01ANLCZnCtq9zBLLXbTMEAqn
```
python3 << 'PYEOF'
import math
from scipy.special import iv  # Modified Bessel function

def skellam_pmf(k, mu1, mu2):
    """P(X1-X2=k) where X1~Pois(mu1), X2~Pois(mu2)"""
    return math.exp(-(mu1+mu2)) * (mu1/mu2)**(k/2) * iv(abs(k), 2*math.sqrt(mu1*mu2))

def skellam_p_greater(mu1, mu2, max_k=50):
    """P(X1 > X2)"""
    total = 0
    for k in range(1, max_k):
        total += skellam_pmf(k, mu1, mu2)
    return total

def skellam_p_greater_or_equal(mu1, mu2, max_k=50):
    """P(X1 >= X2) = P(X1 > X2) + P(X1 = X2)"""
    return skellam_p_greater(mu1, mu2, max_k) + skellam_pmf(0, mu1, mu2)

def poisson_gte(lam, k):
    """P(X >= k) where X ~ Pois(lam)"""
    prob_less = sum(math.exp(-lam) * lam**j / math.factorial(j) for j in range(k))
    return 1 - prob_less

def vig_adj(p, total):
    return p / total

# ===== MARKET PRICES (VIG-ADJUSTED) =====
print("=" * 60)
print("SUI-BIH MARKET PRICES (VIG-ADJUSTED)")
print("=" * 60)

# FTR
sui_raw, draw_raw, bih_raw = 0.6230, 0.2299, 0.1450
ftr_sum = sui_raw + draw_raw + bih_raw
sui_va = vig_adj(sui_raw, ftr_sum)
draw_va = vig_adj(draw_raw, ftr_sum)
bih_va = vig_adj(bih_raw, ftr_sum)
print(f"\nFTR:  SUI={sui_va:.4f}  Draw={draw_va:.4f}  BIH={bih_va:.4f}")

# Goal totals
over25_raw, under25_raw = 0.5052, 0.4904
ou25_sum = over25_raw + under25_raw
over25_va = vig_adj(over25_raw, ou25_sum)
print(f"O/U 2.5: Over={over25_va:.4f}  Under={1-over25_va:.4f}")

over15_raw, under15_raw = 0.7577, 0.2413
ou15_sum = over15_raw + under15_raw
over15_va = vig_adj(over15_raw, ou15_sum)
print(f"O/U 1.5: Over={over15_va:.4f}  Under={1-over15_va:.4f}")

# BTTS
btts_yes_raw, btts_no_raw = 0.4902, 0.5115
btts_sum = btts_yes_raw + btts_no_raw
btts_yes_va = vig_adj(btts_yes_raw, btts_sum)
print(f"BTTS: Yes={btts_yes_va:.4f}  No={1-btts_yes_va:.4f}")

# BTTS + Over 2.5
btts_over_raw = 0.3707
btts_over_va = vig_adj(btts_over_raw, 0.3707+0.1071+0.1290+0.3880)
print(f"BTTS+O2.5: Yes_Over={btts_over_va:.4f}")

# Penalty
pen_yes_raw, pen_no_raw = 0.3000, 0.7032
pen_sum = pen_yes_raw + pen_no_raw
pen_yes_va = vig_adj(pen_yes_raw, pen_sum)
print(f"Penalty: Yes={pen_yes_va:.4f}")

# 2H Goal totals
h2_over15_raw, h2_under15_raw = 0.4377, 0.5578
h2_sum = h2_over15_raw + h2_under15_raw
h2_over15_va = vig_adj(h2_over15_raw, h2_sum)
print(f"2H O/U 1.5: Over={h2_over15_va:.4f}")

# 2H team goals
sui_2h_over_raw, sui_2h_under_raw = 0.6526, 0.3426
sui_2h_sum = sui_2h_over_raw + sui_2h_under_raw
sui_2h_over_va = vig_adj(sui_2h_over_raw, sui_2h_sum)
sui_2h_lambda = -math.log(1 - sui_2h_over_va)
print(f"2H SUI O/U 0.5 goals: Over={sui_2h_over_va:.4f}  λ_SUI_2H_goals={sui_2h_lambda:.4f}")

bih_2h_over_raw, bih_2h_under_raw = 0.3601, 0.6398
bih_2h_sum = bih_2h_over_raw + bih_2h_under_raw
bih_2h_over_va = vig_adj(bih_2h_over_raw, bih_2h_sum)
bih_2h_lambda = -math.log(1 - bih_2h_over_va)
print(f"2H BIH O/U 0.5 goals: Over={bih_2h_over_va:.4f}  λ_BIH_2H_goals={bih_2h_lambda:.4f}")

# Cards
cards_over25_raw, cards_under25_raw = 0.6095, 0.3659
cards_sum = cards_over25_raw + cards_under25_raw
cards_over25_va = vig_adj(cards_over25_raw, cards_sum)
print(f"Cards O/U 2.5: Over={cards_over25_va:.4f}")

print()
print("=" * 60)
print("DERIVED ESTIMATES")
print("=" * 60)

# ===== Q: Bosnia more fouls than Switzerland =====
print("\n--- Bosnia MORE FOULS than Switzerland ---")
lam_bih_fouls = 17.0  # tournament avg (n=6 WC+WCQ)
lam_sui_fouls = 12.0  # tournament avg blended 
p_bih_more_fouls = skellam_p_greater(lam_bih_fouls, lam_sui_fouls)
p_bih_more_fouls_deout = skellam_p_greater(16.2, 11.5)  # de-outlied
print(f"  Skellam P(BIH>SUI): full={p_bih_more_fouls:.4f}  de-outlied={p_bih_more_fouls_deout:.4f}")
print(f"  Draw price: {draw_va:.3f} (RULE8 threshold=0.25 → {'FIRES' if draw_va >= 0.25 else 'does not fire'})")
print(f"  RECOMMENDED: ~0.75 (signal robust, direct no-market prop)")

# ===== Q: Switzerland 2+ offsides =====
print("\n--- Switzerland 2+ OFFSIDES ---")
lam_sui_offs_recent = 1.44  # recent n=9 avg
lam_sui_offs_tournament = 1.67  # tournament avg
p_sui_2plus_recent = poisson_gte(lam_sui_offs_recent, 2)
p_sui_2plus_tournament = poisson_gte(lam_sui_offs_tournament, 2)
p_sui_1offs_wc = poisson_gte(1.0, 2)  # WC vs Qatar: 1 offside (single data point)
print(f"  Poisson P(X>=2): recent λ={lam_sui_offs_recent} → {p_sui_2plus_recent:.4f}")
print(f"  Poisson P(X>=2): tournament λ={lam_sui_offs_tournament} → {p_sui_2plus_tournament:.4f}")
print(f"  Note: WC R1 vs Qatar = 1 offside (DOES NOT fire as 9/9 NO - SUI is ATTACKER)")
print(f"  RECOMMENDED: ~0.44")

# ===== Q: Bosnia 2+ offsides =====
print("\n--- Bosnia 2+ OFFSIDES ---")
lam_bih_offs = 0.0  # ALL ZERO in 6 matches
p_bih_2plus_floor = poisson_gte(0.25, 2)  # floor prior
p_bih_2plus_tiny = poisson_gte(0.10, 2)
print(f"  RAW DATA: 0 offsides in all 6 matches (5 WCQ + WC vs Canada)")
print(f"  Floor λ=0.25: P(X>=2)={p_bih_2plus_floor:.4f}")
print(f"  Floor λ=0.10: P(X>=2)={p_bih_2plus_tiny:.4f}")
print(f"  RECOMMENDED: ~0.04 (EXTREMELY LOW - our most confident extreme)")

# ===== Q: BTTS + 3+ goals =====
print("\n--- BTTS + 3+ GOALS ---")
print(f"  Market (Smarkets): BTTS+Over2.5 Yes = {btts_over_va:.4f}")
print(f"  RECOMMENDED: {btts_over_va:.2f}")

# ===== Q: 2H Over 1.5 goals =====
print("\n--- 2H OVER 1.5 GOALS ---")
h2_total_lambda = sui_2h_lambda + bih_2h_lambda
p_2h_over15_poisson = poisson_gte(h2_total_lambda, 2)
print(f"  Market: 2H Over 1.5 = {h2_over15_va:.4f}")
print(f"  Poisson crosscheck: λ_SUI_2H={sui_2h_lambda:.3f} + λ_BIH_2H={bih_2h_lambda:.3f} = {h2_total_lambda:.3f}")
print(f"  P(2H goals >=2) = {p_2h_over15_poisson:.4f}")
print(f"  RECOMMENDED: {h2_over15_va:.2f}")

# ===== Q: SUI more 2H SOT than BIH =====
print("\n--- SUI MORE 2H SOT THAN BIH ---")
# Market-implied: SUI λ_2H goals = 1.066, BIH λ_2H goals = 0.446
# For SOT: use ESPN. SUI avg 5.0 SOT full, BIH had 3 SOT vs Canada (outpossessed)
# Expected BIH SOT vs SUI: even fewer, λ_BIH_SOT_full ~ 3.0 (vs Canada) → 2.5 more likely
lam_sui_sot_2h = 5.0 / 2  # 2.5
lam_bih_sot_2h = 3.0 / 2  # 1.5 (de-outlied for underdog against dominant attacker)
p_sui_more_sot_2h = skellam_p_greater(lam_sui_sot_2h, lam_bih_sot_2h)
# More aggressive: BIH λ_2H = 1.0 (only 3 SOT total vs Canada, attacking 2H half)
p_sui_more_sot_aggressive = skellam_p_greater(lam_sui_sot_2h, 1.0)
print(f"  ESPN Skellam (λ_SUI={lam_sui_sot_2h}, λ_BIH={lam_bih_sot_2h}): P={p_sui_more_sot_2h:.4f}")
print(f"  ESPN Skellam (λ_SUI={lam_sui_sot_2h}, λ_BIH=1.0): P={p_sui_more_sot_aggressive:.4f}")
# Market sanity: SUI 2H goal lambda=1.066 vs BIH=0.446 → SUI dominates in attack
print(f"  Market goal lambdas: SUI={sui_2h_lambda:.3f} vs BIH={bih_2h_lambda:.3f} (ratio {sui_2h_lambda/bih_2h_lambda:.2f}x)")
print(f"  RECOMMENDED: ~0.68 (between de-outlied and aggressive estimates)")

# ===== Q: Penalty or red card =====
print("\n--- PENALTY OR RED CARD ---")
p_penalty = pen_yes_va
# RC base rate for competitive international: ~10-12%
# BIH had 3 YC vs Canada → elevated RC risk, call it 15%
p_red_card = 0.15
p_either = p_penalty + p_red_card - p_penalty * p_red_card
print(f"  Penalty market: {p_penalty:.4f}")
print(f"  RC estimate (BIH elevated from 3 YC vs CAN): {p_red_card:.2f}")
print(f"  P(pen OR RC) = {p_either:.4f}")
print(f"  RECOMMENDED: ~0.38")

print(f"  RULE1: use market directly. RECOMMENDED: {sui_va:.2f}")

import subprocess, json

# Fetch player SOT quotes
r = subprocess.run(['curl','-sk',
    'https://api.smarkets.com/v3/markets/145290456/quotes/'],
    capture_output=True, text=True)
quotes = json.loads(r.stdout)

key_players = {
    "405446768": "Embolo",
    "405446752": "Dan Ndoye",
    "405446759": "Zeki Amdouni",
    "405446749": "Noah Okafor",
    "405446793": "Edin Dzeko",
    "405446811": "Ermedin Demirovic",
    "405446804": "Haris Tabakovic",
}

print("PLAYER SOT (Over 0.5) quotes:")
for cid, name in key_players.items():
    q = quotes.get(cid, {})
    bids = q.get('bids', [])
    offers = q.get('offers', [])
    bid_price = bids[0]['price'] if bids else None
    offer_price = offers[0]['price'] if offers else None
    bid_pct = bid_price/10000 if bid_price else None
    offer_pct = offer_price/10000 if offer_price else None
    mid = (bid_pct+offer_pct)/2 if (bid_pct and offer_pct) else (offer_pct or bid_pct)
    liq = "liquid" if (bid_pct and offer_pct) else ("offer-only" if offer_pct else "no-quote")
    mid_str = f"{mid:.4f}" if mid else "N/A"
    bid_str = f"{bid_pct:.4f}" if bid_pct else "N/A"
    offer_str = f"{offer_pct:.4f}" if offer_pct else "N/A"
    print(f"  {name}: bid={bid_str} offer={offer_str} mid={mid_str} [{liq}]")

# Red card market
print("\nRed card (any player sent off - 137949961):")
r2 = subprocess.run(['curl','-sk', 'https://api.smarkets.com/v3/markets/137949961/contracts/'], capture_output=True, text=True)
r3 = subprocess.run(['curl','-sk', 'https://api.smarkets.com/v3/markets/137949961/quotes/'], capture_output=True, text=True)

    offers = qt.get('offers', [])

    o = offers[0]['price']/10000 if offers else None
    m = (b+o)/2 if (b and o) else (o or b)
    print(f"  {c['name']}: mid={m:.4f if m else 'N/A'}")

    c4 = json.loads(r4.stdout)

import subprocess, json

def get_market_quotes(mid_id):
    r1 = subprocess.run(['curl','-sk', f'https://api.smarkets.com/v3/markets/{mid_id}/contracts/'], capture_output=True, text=True)
    r2 = subprocess.run(['curl','-sk', f'https://api.smarkets.com/v3/markets/{mid_id}/quotes/'], capture_output=True, text=True)
    contracts = {c['id']: c['name'] for c in json.loads(r1.stdout).get('contracts', [])}
    quotes = json.loads(r2.stdout)
    results = {}
    for cid, cname in contracts.items():
        q = quotes.get(cid, {})
        bids = q.get('bids', [])
        offers = q.get('offers', [])
        b = bids[0]['price']/10000 if bids else None
        o = offers[0]['price']/10000 if offers else None
        m = (b+o)/2 if (b and o) else (o or b)
        results[cname] = {'bid': b, 'offer': o, 'mid': m}
    return results

def fmt(v):
    return f"{v:.4f}" if v is not None else "N/A"

print("Red card (137949961):")
for name, v in get_market_quotes("137949961").items():
    print(f"  {name}: bid={fmt(v['bid'])} offer={fmt(v['offer'])} mid={fmt(v['mid'])}")

print("\nCards Asian Handicap SUI+0.5/BIH-0.5 (137949904):")
for name, v in get_market_quotes("137949904").items():
    print(f"  {name}: mid={fmt(v['mid'])}")

print("\nMost cards market (137949840):")
for name, v in get_market_quotes("137949840").items():
    print(f"  {name}: mid={fmt(v['mid'])}")

import math
from scipy.special import iv

def skellam_p_greater(mu1, mu2, max_k=60):
    total = 0
    for k in range(1, max_k):
        total += math.exp(-(mu1+mu2)) * (mu1/mu2)**(k/2) * iv(k, 2*math.sqrt(mu1*mu2))
    return total

def poisson_gte(lam, k):
    return 1 - sum(math.exp(-lam)*lam**j/math.factorial(j) for j in range(k))

# Illiquid offer adjustment factor
ILLIQUID_FACTOR = 0.945

# DESC: Fetch SportsPredict questions via API

python3 << 'PYEOF'
import subprocess, json

match_id = "cc68a00e-06cd-4fec-9f22-c22ecbe9e39a"
market_id = "801c0468-352b-416a-b329-25ee20c2d849"
event_id = "aa5572ec-5930-4d99-b06b-f8966333d172"

# Try the API endpoints we've used before
urls = [
    f"https://play.sportspredict.com/api/v1/markets/{market_id}/questions",
    f"https://play.sportspredict.com/api/v1/matches/{match_id}/markets/{market_id}",
    f"https://play.sportspredict.com/api/v1/probability-events/{event_id}/markets/{market_id}",
    f"https://play.sportspredict.com/api/markets/{market_id}",
    f"https://api.sportspredict.com/v1/markets/{market_id}/questions",
]

for url in urls:
    r = subprocess.run(['curl', '-sk', '-H', 'Accept: application/json', url],
                       capture_output=True, text=True, timeout=10)
    if r.stdout and len(r.stdout) > 10:
        try:
            d = json.loads(r.stdout)
            print(f"URL: {url}")
            print(json.dumps(d, indent=2)[:1500])
            print("---")
        except:
            print(f"URL: {url} → non-JSON: {r.stdout[:200]}")
PYEOF

import subprocess, json

match_id = "cc68a00e-06cd-4fec-9f22-c22ecbe9e39a"
market_id = "801c0468-352b-416a-b329-25ee20c2d849"

# The API base is api.sportspredict.com - try more endpoints
urls = [
    f"https://api.sportspredict.com/v1/markets/{market_id}",
    f"https://api.sportspredict.com/v1/probability-events/{event_id}/markets",
    f"https://api.sportspredict.com/v1/matches/{match_id}",
    f"https://api.sportspredict.com/v1/matches/{match_id}/markets",
    f"https://api.sportspredict.com/v1/probability-events/{event_id}",
]

for url in urls:
    r = subprocess.run(['curl', '-sk', '-H', 'Accept: application/json',
                        '-H', 'Content-Type: application/json', url],
                       capture_output=True, text=True, timeout=10)
    if r.stdout:
        try:
            d = json.loads(r.stdout)
            print(f"\nURL: {url}")
            print(json.dumps(d, indent=2)[:2000])
        except:
            print(f"\nURL: {url} → {r.stdout[:100]}")

### CMD #50
# DESC: Read the existing SportsPredict fetch bot for working API patterns
# ID: toolu_01MN3six33gQrvH1LYQRBD29
```
cat /Users/aki/Desktop/QK\ Rstudio/sportspredict_research/bot/fetch_smarkets_mapping.py
```

### OUT
"""
Build a one-time mapping of Smarkets World Cup 2026 events -> their full
market list (id + name only, no prices) for all 71 fixtures.

This is metadata-only (cheap: 1 call for the event list + 1 call per match
for its ~200 markets = ~72 calls total). Live prices are fetched separately,
on demand, by fetch_smarkets_prices.py using the market ids saved here.

Output: bot/data/external/smarkets_markets_by_match.jsonl
  one line per match: {"event_id", "name", "start_date", "markets": [{"id","name"}, ...]}

Usage:
    python3 fetch_smarkets_mapping.py
"""

import json
import time
from pathlib import Path

import requests

ROOT = Path(__file__).resolve().parent
OUT_DIR = ROOT / "data" / "external"
OUT_DIR.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
OUT_PATH = OUT_DIR / "smarkets_markets_by_match.jsonl"

BASE = "https://api.smarkets.com/v3"
WC2026_PARENT_ID = "42791414"


def main():
    resp = requests.get(f"{BASE}/events/", params={
        "type": "football_match", "parent_id": WC2026_PARENT_ID, "limit": 1000
    }, timeout=30)
    resp.raise_for_status()
    events = resp.json()["events"]
    print(f"Found {len(events)} WC2026 events")

    done_ids = set()
    if OUT_PATH.exists():
        with open(OUT_PATH) as f:
            for line in f:
                done_ids.add(json.loads(line)["event_id"])
        print(f"Resuming: {len(done_ids)} already fetched")

    with open(OUT_PATH, "a") as out:
        for i, e in enumerate(events):
            if e["id"] in done_ids:
                continue
            mr = requests.get(f"{BASE}/events/{e['id']}/markets/",
                               params={"limit": 1000}, timeout=30)
            mr.raise_for_status()
            markets = [{"id": m["id"], "name": m["name"]} for m in mr.json()["markets"]]
            out.write(json.dumps({
                "event_id": e["id"],
                "name": e["name"],
                "start_date": e["start_date"],
                "markets": markets,
            }) + "\n")
            out.flush()
            print(f"[{i+1}/{len(events)}] {e['name']}: {len(markets)} markets")
            time.sleep(0.3)

    print(f"Wrote mapping to {OUT_PATH}")


if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
------------------------------------------------------------

### CMD #56
# DESC: Fetch Xhaka player SOT quote and derive 2H probability
# ID: toolu_017S5N9TFzo7pKb8xc9BS3xo
```
python3 << 'PYEOF'
import subprocess, json, math
from scipy.special import iv

# Fetch Xhaka quote from player SOT market
r = subprocess.run(['curl','-sk','https://api.smarkets.com/v3/markets/145290456/quotes/'],
                   capture_output=True, text=True)
quotes = json.loads(r.stdout)

xhaka_cid = "405446765"
q = quotes.get(xhaka_cid, {})
bids = q.get('bids', [])
offers = q.get('offers', [])
bid = bids[0]['price']/10000 if bids else None
offer = offers[0]['price']/10000 if offers else None
mid = (bid+offer)/2 if (bid and offer) else (offer or bid)
liq = "liquid" if (bid and offer) else ("offer-only" if offer else "no-quote")
print(f"Xhaka full-match SOT: bid={bid} offer={offer} mid={mid} [{liq}]")

# Derive 2H estimate
if mid:
    lam_full = -math.log(1 - mid)
    lam_2h = lam_full / 2
    p_2h = 1 - math.exp(-lam_2h)
    print(f"  λ_full={lam_full:.4f} → λ_2H={lam_2h:.4f} → P(1+ SOT in 2H)={p_2h:.4f}")
elif offer:
    adj = offer * 0.945  # illiquid adjustment
    lam_full = -math.log(1 - adj)
    lam_2h = lam_full / 2
    p_2h = 1 - math.exp(-lam_2h)
    print(f"  illiquid_adj={adj:.4f} → λ_2H={lam_2h:.4f} → P(1+ SOT in 2H)={p_2h:.4f}")

# Also check Amdouni for reference (Q9 backup awareness)
amdouni_cid = "405446759"
q2 = quotes.get(amdouni_cid, {})
offers2 = q2.get('offers', [])
offer2 = offers2[0]['price']/10000 if offers2 else None
print(f"\nAmdouni full-match SOT: offer={offer2}")

# Also check if there's a market 145290458 (over 1.5 SOT) that could give us Xhaka's lambda
# Let me check the 2H SOT specific market or shots market
print("\n--- Checking other shot markets ---")
for mid_id in ["145290462", "145290464"]:  # Over 0.5 shots, over 1.5 shots (not SOT)
    r2 = subprocess.run(['curl','-sk', f'https://api.smarkets.com/v3/markets/{mid_id}/quotes/'],
                        capture_output=True, text=True)
    q2 = json.loads(r2.stdout)
    xq = q2.get(xhaka_cid, {})
    o = xq.get('offers', [{}])[0].get('price',0)/10000 if xq.get('offers') else None
    b = xq.get('bids', [{}])[0].get('price',0)/10000 if xq.get('bids') else None
    print(f"  Market {mid_id}, Xhaka: bid={b} offer={o}")

import math
from scipy.special import iv

def skellam_p_greater(mu1, mu2, max_k=60):
    total = 0
    for k in range(1, max_k):
        total += math.exp(-(mu1+mu2)) * (mu1/mu2)**(k/2) * iv(k, 2*math.sqrt(mu1*mu2))
    return total

def poisson_gte(lam, k):
    return 1 - sum(math.exp(-lam)*lam**j/math.factorial(j) for j in range(k))

ILLIQUID = 0.945

import subprocess, json

# Try ESPN API for referee and lineup data
r = subprocess.run(['curl','-sk',
    'https://site.api.espn.com/apis/site/v2/sports/soccer/fifa.world/summary?event=760439'],
    capture_output=True, text=True)

# Look for officials/referee

print("=== OFFICIALS/REFEREE ===")
if officials:
    for o in officials:
        print(json.dumps(o, indent=2))
else:
    print("No officials found in gameInfo")
    print("gameInfo keys:", list(d.get('gameInfo',{}).keys()))

# Look for rosters/lineups
print("\n=== ROSTERS/LINEUPS ===")
rosters = d.get('rosters', [])
if rosters:
    for team in rosters:
        tname = team.get('team', {}).get('displayName', 'Unknown')
        print(f"\n{tname}:")
        athletes = team.get('roster', [])
        for a in athletes:
            name = a.get('athlete', {}).get('displayName', '?')
            starter = a.get('starter', False)
            position = a.get('position', {}).get('abbreviation', '?')
            status = a.get('playingStatus', {})
            print(f"  {'[START]' if starter else '[BENCH]'} {name} ({position})")
else:
    print("No rosters field found")
    print("Top-level keys:", list(d.keys())[:20])

import subprocess

# Try FBRef/football-reference for WC2026 match data
urls = [
    "https://fbref.com/en/comps/1/schedule/World-Cup-Scores-and-Fixtures",
    "https://www.transfermarkt.com/weltmeisterschaft-2026/gesamtspielplan/pokalwettbewerb/WM26",
]
for url in urls:
    r = subprocess.run(['curl','-sk','-L','-A','Mozilla/5.0',
                        '--max-time','10', url],
                       capture_output=True, text=True)
    # Look for referee mentions and SUI/BIH
    lines = r.stdout.split('\n')
    for i, line in enumerate(lines):
        if any(kw in line.lower() for kw in ['referee', 'official', 'switzerland', 'bosnia']):
            if 'referee' in line.lower() or ('switzerland' in line.lower() and 'bosnia' in line.lower()):
                print(f"[{url[:40]}] Line {i}: {line[:200]}")

# DESC: Dig deeper into ESPN API for referee data
# ID: toolu_011zu7tTAp6eDpEJZEKTh1VW
```
python3 << 'PYEOF'
import subprocess, json

# Try broader ESPN API fields
r = subprocess.run(['curl','-sk',
    'https://site.api.espn.com/apis/site/v2/sports/soccer/fifa.world/summary?event=760439'],
    capture_output=True, text=True)
d = json.loads(r.stdout)

# Scan all top-level keys for any referee info
for key in d.keys():
    val = d[key]
    val_str = json.dumps(val)
    if 'referee' in val_str.lower() or 'official' in val_str.lower():
        print(f"Found in key '{key}':", val_str[:500])

# Also try the header/boxscore
header = d.get('header', {})
comps = header.get('competitions', [{}])[0] if header.get('competitions') else {}
print("\nCompetition keys:", list(comps.keys()))

### CMD #65
# DESC: Compute final revised estimates with referee and lineup adjustments

import math
from scipy.special import iv

def skellam_p_greater(mu1, mu2, max_k=60):
    total = 0
    for k in range(1, max_k):
        total += math.exp(-(mu1+mu2)) * (mu1/mu2)**(k/2) * iv(k, 2*math.sqrt(mu1*mu2))
    return total

def poisson_gte(lam, k):
    return 1 - sum(math.exp(-lam)*lam**j/math.factorial(j) for j in range(k))

print("=" * 70)
print("SUI vs BIH — REVISED SUBMISSION (WITH REFEREE + LINEUP DATA)")

  - vs league average: YC rate ~32% ABOVE average (avg ~3.5/game)

### CMD #69
# DESC: Find CAN-QAT ESPN event ID
# ID: toolu_01QtDEXK2SoMhB8qKBXRQhqK
```
python3 << 'PYEOF'
import subprocess, json

# Find CAN-QAT ESPN event ID (scan from 760440 upward)
print("Scanning for CAN-QAT ESPN event ID...")
for eid in range(760440, 760460):
    r = subprocess.run(['curl','-sk','--max-time','4',
        f'https://site.api.espn.com/apis/site/v2/sports/soccer/fifa.world/summary?event={eid}'],
        capture_output=True, text=True)
    if not r.stdout: continue
    try:
        d = json.loads(r.stdout)
        comps = d.get('header',{}).get('competitions',[{}])[0]
        competitors = comps.get('competitors',[])
        names = [c.get('team',{}).get('abbreviation','?') for c in competitors]
        date = comps.get('date','?')[:10]
        status = comps.get('status',{}).get('type',{}).get('description','?')
        if any(n in ['CAN','QAT','Canada','Qatar'] for n in names):
            print(f"  eid={eid}: {names}  {date}  {status}  ← FOUND!")
            break
        else:
            print(f"  eid={eid}: {names}  {date}")
    except: pass
PYEOF
```

### CMD #73
# DESC: Load existing Canada and Qatar ESPN data from saved files
# ID: toolu_011VPXfWu4YqmTFe6pH2NUaa
```
python3 << 'PYEOF'
import subprocess, json

# Fetch Canada and Qatar recent ESPN stats 
# First check what we already have saved
import os, glob
data_dir = '/Users/aki/Desktop/QK Rstudio/sportspredict_research/data/external_markets/'
for fname in ['can_bih_2026-06-12.json', 'qat_sui_2026-06-13.json']:
    fpath = data_dir + fname
    if os.path.exists(fpath):
        with open(fpath) as f:
            d = json.load(f)
        print(f"\n=== {fname} ===")
        src = d.get('sources',{})
        for key, val in src.items():
            if 'espn' in key.lower() or 'recent' in key.lower():
                print(f"  {key}:")
                if isinstance(val, dict):
                    avgs = val.get('averages_n4') or val.get('averages_n5') or val.get('averages_n6') or val.get('averages_n8') or val.get('averages_n9')
                    if avgs:
                        print(f"    Averages: {avgs}")
                    matches = val.get('matches') or val.get('matches_n4') or val.get('matches_n5') or val.get('matches_n8') or val.get('matches_n9')
                    if matches:
                        for m in matches[:3]:
                            print(f"    {m}")
PYEOF
```

    "AH_CAN_minus0.5": 137950292,

    if mid is None:
        continue
    r = subprocess.run(['curl','-sk',f'https://api.smarkets.com/v3/markets/{mid}/quotes/'],
        capture_output=True, text=True)

        d = json.loads(r.stdout)
        results[name] = d
    except:
        results[name] = {"error": r.stdout[:200]}

    json.dump(results, f, indent=2)
print("Saved raw quotes")

# Extract key prices
def extract_best_price(quotes_dict, label_hint=None):
    """Returns dict of {contract_id: best_price} as decimal probability"""
    out = {}
    for cid, cdata in quotes_dict.items():
        if not isinstance(cdata, dict):
            continue
        # Try offer side (lowest offer = best price for buyer = market implied prob)
        offers = cdata.get('offers', [])
        bids = cdata.get('bids', [])
        if offers:
            best_offer = min(int(x[0]) for x in offers) / 10000
            out[cid] = best_offer
        elif bids:
            best_bid = max(int(x[0]) for x in bids) / 10000
            out[cid] = best_bid
    return out

# FTR
ftr_quotes = results.get('FTR', {}).get('quotes', results.get('FTR', {}))
print("\n=== FTR RAW ===")
print(str(ftr_quotes)[:500])

import subprocess, json

# Fetch Canada recent ESPN data (post-BIH match)
# Try fetching Canada WC2026 R1 stats from ESPN
def espn_event_stats(event_id, team_name):
    r = subprocess.run(['curl','-sk',
        f'https://site.api.espn.com/apis/site/v2/sports/soccer/fifa.world/summary?event={event_id}'],
        capture_output=True, text=True)
    d = json.loads(r.stdout)
    
    # Get team stats
    comps = d.get('header',{}).get('competitions',[{}])[0]
    result = {}
    for comp in d.get('header',{}).get('competitions',[]):
        pass
    
    # boxscore stats
    for b in d.get('boxscore',{}).get('teams',[]):
        tname = b.get('team',{}).get('displayName','?')
        if team_name.lower() in tname.lower():
            stats = {}
            for s in b.get('statistics',[]):
                stats[s.get('name','')] = s.get('displayValue','')
            result[tname] = stats
    return result

# Canada vs Bosnia (760438?) - need right id
# Let's search for recent Canada matches

    'https://site.api.espn.com/apis/site/v2/sports/soccer/fifa.world/teams/6?limit=10'],
    capture_output=True, text=True)
d = json.loads(r.stdout)

### CMD #80
# DESC: Fetch all CAN-QAT Smarkets markets with contract names and parsed prices
# ID: toolu_018jKybY2om2N5tGMMKLbiia
```
python3 << 'PYEOF'
import subprocess, json

# Get all contracts and quotes for key markets at once
def get_market_with_contracts(market_id):
    r = subprocess.run(['curl','-sk',
        f'https://api.smarkets.com/v3/markets/{market_id}/contracts/'],
        capture_output=True, text=True)
    try:
        contracts = {c['id']: c['name'] for c in json.loads(r.stdout).get('contracts',[])}
    except:
        contracts = {}
    
    r2 = subprocess.run(['curl','-sk',
        f'https://api.smarkets.com/v3/markets/{market_id}/quotes/'],
        capture_output=True, text=True)
    try:
        quotes = json.loads(r2.stdout)
    except:
        quotes = {}
    
    result = {}
    for cid, prices in quotes.items():
        name = contracts.get(cid, cid)
        offers = prices.get('offers', [])
        bids = prices.get('bids', [])
        best_offer = min(int(x['price'] if isinstance(x,dict) else x[0]) for x in offers) / 10000 if offers else None
        best_bid = max(int(x['price'] if isinstance(x,dict) else x[0]) for x in bids) / 10000 if bids else None
        # mid or best price
        if best_offer and best_bid:
            mid = (best_offer + best_bid) / 2
        elif best_offer:
            mid = best_offer * 0.945  # illiquid adjustment
        elif best_bid:
            mid = best_bid
        else:
            mid = None
        result[name] = {'offer': best_offer, 'bid': best_bid, 'mid_adj': mid}
    return result

markets_to_fetch = {
    'FTR': 137950209,
    'BTTS': 137950211,
    'OU2.5': 137950246,
    'OU1.5': 137950245,
    'Penalty': 137950234,
    '2H_result': 137950215,
    '2H_OU1.5': 137950255,
    '2H_OU0.5': 137950254,
    '2H_CAN_OU0.5': 137950264,
    '2H_QAT_OU0.5': 137950274,
    'Cards_OU1.5': 137950362,
    'Cards_OU2.5': 137950364,
    'AH_CAN_minus0.5': 137950292,
    'QAT_corners_OU3.5': 137950388,
    'QAT_corners_OU4.5': 137950390,
    'CAN_corners_OU5.5': 137950391,
    'CAN_SOT_OU4.5': 143916368,
    'QAT_SOT_OU2.5': 143916414,
    'PlayerSOT_0.5plus': 145291620,
    'Most_cards': 137950233,
}

all_results = {}
for name, mid in markets_to_fetch.items():
    print(f"Fetching {name}...", end=' ', flush=True)
    res = get_market_with_contracts(mid)
    all_results[name] = res
    # Print key numbers
    for contract_name, prices in res.items():
        if prices['mid_adj']:
            print(f"\n  {contract_name}: {prices['mid_adj']:.4f}", end='')
    print()

# Save to disk immediately
with open('/Users/aki/Desktop/QK Rstudio/sportspredict_research/data/external_markets/can_qat_smarkets_parsed.json','w') as f:
    json.dump(all_results, f, indent=2)
print("\nSaved parsed quotes")

### CMD #81
# DESC: Fetch and parse all CAN-QAT Smarkets market prices with contract names
# ID: toolu_01CDTBz9CvZMZqZcg5TAdKhR
```
python3 << 'PYEOF'
import subprocess, json

def get_market_prices(market_id):
    # Get contracts
    r = subprocess.run(['curl','-sk',
        f'https://api.smarkets.com/v3/markets/{market_id}/contracts/'],
        capture_output=True, text=True)
    contracts = {str(c['id']): c['name'] for c in json.loads(r.stdout).get('contracts',[])}
    
    # Get quotes
    r2 = subprocess.run(['curl','-sk',
        f'https://api.smarkets.com/v3/markets/{market_id}/quotes/'],
        capture_output=True, text=True)
    raw = json.loads(r2.stdout)
    
    result = {}
    for cid, prices in raw.items():
        if not isinstance(prices, dict):
            continue
        name = contracts.get(str(cid), str(cid))
        # prices format: {'bids': [[price, qty], ...], 'offers': [[price, qty], ...]}
        offers = prices.get('offers', [])
        bids = prices.get('bids', [])
        
        def get_best(lst, fn):
            try:
                vals = []
                for x in lst:
                    if isinstance(x, (list, tuple)):
                        vals.append(int(x[0]))
                    elif isinstance(x, dict):
                        vals.append(int(x.get('price', x.get('p', 0))))
                return fn(vals) / 10000 if vals else None
            except:
                return None
        
        best_offer = get_best(offers, min)
        best_bid = get_best(bids, max)
        
        if best_offer and best_bid:
            mid = (best_offer + best_bid) / 2
            liquid = True
        elif best_offer:
            mid = best_offer * 0.945
            liquid = False
        elif best_bid:
            mid = best_bid
            liquid = False
        else:
            mid = None
            liquid = False
        
        result[name] = {'offer': best_offer, 'bid': best_bid, 'mid': mid, 'liquid': liquid}
    return result

markets = {
    'FTR': 137950209,
    'OU2.5': 137950246,
    'OU1.5': 137950245,
    'Penalty': 137950234,
    '2H_result': 137950215,
    '2H_OU1.5': 137950255,
    '2H_OU0.5': 137950254,
    '2H_CAN_OU0.5': 137950264,
    '2H_QAT_OU0.5': 137950274,
    'Cards_OU1.5': 137950362,
    'Cards_OU2.5': 137950364,
    'AH_CAN_minus0.5': 137950292,
    'QAT_corners_OU4.5': 137950390,
    'QAT_corners_OU3.5': 137950388,
    'CAN_SOT_OU4.5': 143916368,
    'QAT_SOT_OU2.5': 143916414,
    'PlayerSOT_0.5plus': 145291620,
    'Most_cards': 137950233,
    'BTTS': 137950211,
}

all_results = {}
for name, mid in markets.items():
    res = get_market_prices(mid)
    all_results[name] = res
    print(f"\n{name}:")
    for cname, p in res.items():
        if p['mid']:
            liq = "liquid" if p['liquid'] else "illiq"
            print(f"  {cname}: mid={p['mid']:.4f} [{liq}]")

with open('/Users/aki/Desktop/QK Rstudio/sportspredict_research/data/external_markets/can_qat_smarkets_parsed.json','w') as f:
    json.dump(all_results, f, indent=2)
print("\n\n=== SAVED ===")
PYEOF
```

### CMD #82
# DESC: Find ESPN event IDs for CAN-BIH and other WC2026 matches
# ID: toolu_014MSoc6DmTfWxB3CQ7J2C8H
```
python3 << 'PYEOF'
import subprocess, json

# Fetch Canada recent matches from ESPN
# Canada team id = 206 in men's national team context
# Let's look for their WC2026 data + recent friendlies

# First, get CAN-BIH match (760438 is a guess based on ESPN event IDs around 760439/760440)
# We know 760439=SUI-BIH and 760440=CAN-QAT
# CAN-BIH was round 1, try nearby IDs
event_ids_to_try = [760438, 760437, 760436, 760435, 760433]
for eid in event_ids_to_try:
    r = subprocess.run(['curl','-sk',
        f'https://site.api.espn.com/apis/site/v2/sports/soccer/fifa.world/summary?event={eid}'],
        capture_output=True, text=True)
    try:
        d = json.loads(r.stdout)
        comps = d.get('header',{}).get('competitions',[{}])[0]
        teams = [c['team']['displayName'] for c in comps.get('competitors',[])]
        status = comps.get('status',{}).get('type',{}).get('description','?')
        date = comps.get('date','?')
        print(f"Event {eid}: {' vs '.join(teams)} - {status} - {date}")
    except:
        print(f"Event {eid}: parse error")
PYEOF
```

### CMD #86
# DESC: Fetch CAN-BIH ESPN match stats for Canada
# ID: toolu_016DtZ2iVpECPHqg5a5SGssB
```
python3 << 'PYEOF'
import subprocess, json

def get_team_stats(event_id, team_hint=''):
    r = subprocess.run(['curl','-sk',
        f'https://site.api.espn.com/apis/site/v2/sports/soccer/fifa.world/summary?event={event_id}'],
        capture_output=True, text=True)
    d = json.loads(r.stdout)
    
    comps = d.get('header',{}).get('competitions',[{}])[0]
    date = comps.get('date','?')[:10]
    teams = {c['team']['displayName']: c for c in comps.get('competitors',[])}
    
    print(f"\nEvent {event_id} ({date}): {' vs '.join(teams.keys())}")
    
    for b in d.get('boxscore',{}).get('teams',[]):
        tname = b.get('team',{}).get('displayName','?')
        stats = {}
        for s in b.get('statistics',[]):
            stats[s.get('name','')] = s.get('displayValue','')
        fouls = stats.get('fouls','?')
        sot = stats.get('shotsOnTarget','?')
        shots = stats.get('totalShots','?')
        poss = stats.get('possessionPct','?')
        offsides = stats.get('offsides','?')
        corners = stats.get('corners','?')
        yc = stats.get('yellowCards','?')
        rc = stats.get('redCards','?')
        print(f"  {tname}: fouls={fouls}, sot={sot}, shots={shots}, poss={poss}%, offsides={offsides}, corners={corners}, YC={yc}, RC={rc}")

# CAN-BIH (Canada vs Bosnia)
get_team_stats(760416)
# QAT-SUI R1: need to find - check nearby IDs around June 13
PYEOF
```

### CMD #92
# DESC: Find halftime result market ID for CAN-QAT
# ID: toolu_01JDG5fGhTyh6o4y5fGBhMZc
```
python3 << 'PYEOF'
import subprocess, json

# Fetch 1H result market for Q6
r = subprocess.run(['curl','-sk','https://api.smarkets.com/v3/events/45042835/markets/'],
    capture_output=True, text=True)
d = json.loads(r.stdout)

# Find half-time markets
ht_markets = []
for m in d.get('markets',[]):
    name = m['name'].lower()
    if 'half-time' in name or 'first half result' in name or 'half time result' in name or 'half-time result' in name:
        ht_markets.append((m['id'], m['name']))

print("HT markets found:")
for mid, name in ht_markets:
    print(f"  [{mid}] {name}")

# Also look for "half" in name
halftime_mids = []
for m in d.get('markets',[]):
    name_lower = m['name'].lower()
    if 'half-time result' in name_lower:
        halftime_mids.append(m['id'])
        print(f"FOUND: [{m['id']}] {m['name']}")
PYEOF
```

### CMD #95
# DESC: Fetch halftime result and 1H AH markets for Q6
# ID: toolu_01BW4KLHZqLxatCL2GzDLBrR
```
python3 << 'PYEOF'
import subprocess, json

# Fetch halftime result market for CAN-QAT
def get_market_prices(market_id):
    r = subprocess.run(['curl','-sk',
        f'https://api.smarkets.com/v3/markets/{market_id}/contracts/'],
        capture_output=True, text=True)
    contracts = {str(c['id']): c['name'] for c in json.loads(r.stdout).get('contracts',[])}
    
    r2 = subprocess.run(['curl','-sk',
        f'https://api.smarkets.com/v3/markets/{market_id}/quotes/'],
        capture_output=True, text=True)
    raw = json.loads(r2.stdout)
    
    result = {}
    for cid, prices in raw.items():
        if not isinstance(prices, dict):
            continue
        name = contracts.get(str(cid), str(cid))
        offers = prices.get('offers', [])
        bids = prices.get('bids', [])
        
        def get_best(lst, fn):
            try:
                vals = [int(x[0] if isinstance(x,(list,tuple)) else x.get('price',0)) for x in lst]
                return fn(vals) / 10000 if vals else None
            except:
                return None
        
        best_offer = get_best(offers, min)
        best_bid = get_best(bids, max)
        
        if best_offer and best_bid:
            mid = (best_offer + best_bid) / 2
            liquid = True
        elif best_offer:
            mid = best_offer * 0.945
            liquid = False
        elif best_bid:
            mid = best_bid
            liquid = False
        else:
            mid = None
            liquid = False
        
        result[name] = {'offer': best_offer, 'bid': best_bid, 'mid': mid, 'liquid': liquid}
    return result

# Halftime result
ht = get_market_prices(137950216)
print("Half-time result:")
for name, p in ht.items():
    print(f"  {name}: mid={p['mid']:.4f}")

# First half AH -0.5 (Canada wins HT)
ah_1h = get_market_prices(137950293)
print("\n1H AH Canada -0.5:")
for name, p in ah_1h.items():
    print(f"  {name}: mid={p['mid']:.4f}")

# First half OU 0.5 goals (to check total scoring rate)
fh_goals = get_market_prices(137950252)  # 1H OU1.5
fh_goals2 = get_market_prices(137950264)  # Wait, this is 2H CAN OU 0.5
print("\n1H OU1.5 goals:")
for name, p in fh_goals.items():
    print(f"  {name}: mid={p['mid']:.4f}")
PYEOF
```

### CMD #96
# DESC: Get individual player SOT stats from CAN-BIH boxscore
# ID: toolu_01Xu3DaDD84hfm2Za6PU4T3f
```
python3 << 'PYEOF'
import subprocess, json

# Try to get Jonathan David's individual match stats
# Check ESPN for CAN-BIH and look for individual player stats differently
r = subprocess.run(['curl','-sk',
    'https://site.api.espn.com/apis/site/v2/sports/soccer/fifa.world/summary?event=760416'],
    capture_output=True, text=True)
d = json.loads(r.stdout)

# Check what's in 'boxscore' -> 'players'
players = d.get('boxscore',{}).get('players',[])
print(f"Players sections: {len(players)}")
for p in players:
    tname = p.get('team',{}).get('displayName','?')
    print(f"\n{tname}:")
    for stat_group in p.get('statistics',[]):
        cat = stat_group.get('name','?')
        for athlete in stat_group.get('athletes',[]):
            aname = athlete.get('athlete',{}).get('displayName','?')
            stats = {s.get('name'):s.get('value') for s in athlete.get('stats',[])}
            if any(k in ['shotsOnTarget','shots'] for k in stats):
                sot = stats.get('shotsOnTarget',0)
                shots = stats.get('shots',0)
                if (sot and sot!='0') or (shots and shots!='0'):
                    print(f"  [{cat}] {aname}: SOT={sot}, shots={shots}")
PYEOF
```

### CMD #102
# DESC: Fetch MEX-KOR ESPN lineups and status
# ID: toolu_019BPyhgqnpkzmdixdR4C3b1
```
python3 << 'PYEOF'
import subprocess, json

# ESPN lineups + referee for MEX vs KOR (event 760441)
r = subprocess.run(['curl','-sk',
    'https://site.api.espn.com/apis/site/v2/sports/soccer/fifa.world/summary?event=760441'],
    capture_output=True, text=True)

# Status
comps = d.get('header',{}).get('competitions',[{}])[0]
status = comps.get('status',{}).get('type',{}).get('description','?')
print(f"Match status: {status}")

# Officials
gi = d.get('gameInfo',{})
for official in gi.get('officials',[]):
    print(f"Official: {official.get('displayName')} - {official.get('position',{}).get('displayName','')}")

# Lineups
for team in d.get('rosters', []):
    tname = team.get('team',{}).get('displayName','?')
    print(f"\n{tname}:")
    for a in team.get('roster', []):
        name = a.get('athlete',{}).get('displayName','?')
        pos = a.get('position',{}).get('abbreviation','?')
        starter = a.get('starter', False)
        if starter:
            print(f"  [START] {name} ({pos})")
PYEOF

### CMD #104
# DESC: Fetch all MEX-KOR Smarkets markets with prices
# ID: toolu_01E7aGWsyWH7TV3uTpznzfXF
```
python3 << 'PYEOF'
import subprocess, json

# Fetch key Smarkets markets for MEX-KOR with prices
def get_market_prices(market_id):
    r = subprocess.run(['curl','-sk',
        f'https://api.smarkets.com/v3/markets/{market_id}/contracts/'],
        capture_output=True, text=True)
    contracts = {str(c['id']): c['name'] for c in json.loads(r.stdout).get('contracts',[])}
    
    r2 = subprocess.run(['curl','-sk',
        f'https://api.smarkets.com/v3/markets/{market_id}/quotes/'],
        capture_output=True, text=True)
    raw = json.loads(r2.stdout)
    
    result = {}
    for cid, prices in raw.items():
        if not isinstance(prices, dict):
            continue
        name = contracts.get(str(cid), str(cid))
        offers = prices.get('offers', [])
        bids = prices.get('bids', [])
        
        def get_best(lst, fn):
            try:
                vals = [int(x[0] if isinstance(x,(list,tuple)) else x.get('price',0)) for x in lst]
                return fn(vals) / 10000 if vals else None
            except: return None
        
        best_offer = get_best(offers, min)
        best_bid = get_best(bids, max)
        
        if best_offer and best_bid:
            mid = (best_offer + best_bid) / 2
            liquid = True
        elif best_offer:
            mid = best_offer * 0.945
            liquid = False
        elif best_bid:
            mid = best_bid
            liquid = False
        else:
            mid = None
            liquid = False
        
        result[name] = {'offer': best_offer, 'bid': best_bid, 'mid': mid, 'liquid': liquid}
    return result

markets = {
    'FTR': 137950762,
    'OU2.5': 137950799,
    'OU1.5': 137950798,
    'BTTS': 137950764,
    'Penalty': 137950787,
    'HT_result': 137950769,
    '2H_result': 137950768,
    '2H_OU1.5': 137950808,
    '2H_OU0.5': 137950807,
    '2H_MEX_OU0.5': 137950817,
    '2H_KOR_OU0.5': 137950827,
    'Cards_OU2.5': 137950916,
    'Cards_OU3.5': 137950918,
    'Most_cards': 137950786,
    'AH_MEX_minus0.5': 137950845,
    'KOR_corners_OU3.5': 137950942,
    'KOR_corners_OU4.5': 137950944,
    'MEX_corners_OU3.5': 137950939,
    'MEX_corners_OU4.5': 137950941,
    'Corner_handicap_MEX_minus0.5': 137950882,
    'MEX_SOT_OU4.5': 144135260,
    'KOR_SOT_OU2.5': 144135306,
    'PlayerSOT_0.5plus': 145452817,
}

all_results = {}
for name, mid in markets.items():
    res = get_market_prices(mid)
    all_results[name] = res
    print(f"\n{name}:")
    for cname, p in res.items():
        if p['mid']:
            liq = "L" if p['liquid'] else "I"
            print(f"  {cname}: {p['mid']:.4f} [{liq}]")

with open('/Users/aki/Desktop/QK Rstudio/sportspredict_research/data/external_markets/mex_kor_smarkets_parsed.json','w') as f:
    json.dump(all_results, f, indent=2)
print("\n=== SAVED ===")
PYEOF
```

### CMD #114
# DESC: Fetch Mexico and Korea WC2026 R1 stats from ESPN
# ID: toolu_01PsJ4imvzWyJrFk8w1rNNxa
```
python3 << 'PYEOF'
import subprocess, json

# Fetch Mexico R1 and Korea R1 stats
def get_team_stats(event_id):
    r = subprocess.run(['curl','-sk',
        f'https://site.api.espn.com/apis/site/v2/sports/soccer/fifa.world/summary?event={event_id}'],
        capture_output=True, text=True)
    d = json.loads(r.stdout)
    
    comps = d.get('header',{}).get('competitions',[{}])[0]
    date = comps.get('date','?')[:10]
    teams = [c['team']['displayName'] for c in comps.get('competitors',[])]
    score = '-'.join([c.get('score','?') for c in comps.get('competitors',[])])
    print(f"\nEvent {event_id} ({date}): {' vs '.join(teams)} - FT: {score}")
    
    for b in d.get('boxscore',{}).get('teams',[]):
        tname = b.get('team',{}).get('displayName','?')
        stats = {s.get('name'):s.get('displayValue') for s in b.get('statistics',[])}
        fouls = stats.get('foulsCommitted','?')
        sot = stats.get('shotsOnTarget','?')
        shots = stats.get('totalShots','?')
        poss = stats.get('possessionPct','?')
        offsides = stats.get('offsides','?')
        corners = stats.get('wonCorners','?')
        yc = stats.get('yellowCards','?')
        rc = stats.get('redCards','?')
        print(f"  {tname}: fouls={fouls}, sot={sot}, shots={shots}, poss={poss}%, offsides={offsides}, corners={corners}, YC={yc}, RC={rc}")

# Mexico R1 (vs South Africa)
get_team_stats(760415)
# Korea R1 (vs Czechia)
get_team_stats(760414)
PYEOF
```

python3 << 'PYEOF'
import subprocess, json

# Fetch Felix Zwayer stats from web
r = subprocess.run(['curl','-sk','-L','-A','Mozilla/5.0',
    '-H','Accept: text/html',
    'https://www.worldfootball.net/schiedsrichter/felix-zwayer/'],
    capture_output=True)
try:
    text = r.stdout.decode('latin-1', errors='replace')
    # Find relevant stats
    import re
    # look for yellow card data
    for match in re.finditer(r'(gelb|yellow|karte|card)', text.lower()):
        print(text[max(0,match.start()-100):match.end()+200])
        print('---')
        break
except:
    print("decode error")

# Try soccerway for Zwayer
r2 = subprocess.run(['curl','-sk','-A','Mozilla/5.0',
    'https://int.soccerway.com/referees/felix-zwayer/'],
    capture_output=True, text=True)
print(r2.stdout[:500])

def get_market_prices(market_id):
    r = subprocess.run(['curl','-sk',
        f'https://api.smarkets.com/v3/markets/{market_id}/contracts/'],
        capture_output=True, text=True)
    contracts = {str(c['id']): c['name'] for c in json.loads(r.stdout).get('contracts',[])}
    r2 = subprocess.run(['curl','-sk',
        f'https://api.smarkets.com/v3/markets/{market_id}/quotes/'],
        capture_output=True, text=True)
    raw = json.loads(r2.stdout)
    result = {}
    for cid, prices in raw.items():
        if not isinstance(prices, dict): continue
        name = contracts.get(str(cid), str(cid))
        offers = prices.get('offers', [])
        bids = prices.get('bids', [])
        def get_best(lst, fn):
            try:
                vals = [int(x[0] if isinstance(x,(list,tuple)) else x.get('price',0)) for x in lst]
                return fn(vals) / 10000 if vals else None
            except: return None
        best_offer = get_best(offers, min)
        best_bid = get_best(bids, max)
        if best_offer and best_bid:
            mid = (best_offer + best_bid) / 2; liquid = True
        elif best_offer:
            mid = best_offer * 0.945; liquid = False
        elif best_bid:
            mid = best_bid; liquid = False
        else:
            mid = None; liquid = False
        result[name] = {'offer': best_offer, 'bid': best_bid, 'mid': mid, 'liquid': liquid}
    return result

# Player SOT 0.5+ market
player_sot = get_market_prices(145452817)
print("Player SOT >0.5 (sorted by mid desc):")
sorted_players = sorted([(n, p) for n, p in player_sot.items() if p['mid']], 
                         key=lambda x: x[1]['mid'], reverse=True)
for name, p in sorted_players:
    liq = "L" if p['liquid'] else "I"
    print(f"  {name}: {p['mid']:.4f} [{liq}]")
PYEOF
```

import subprocess, json

def get_market_prices(market_id):
    r = subprocess.run(['curl','-sk',
        f'https://api.smarkets.com/v3/markets/{market_id}/contracts/'],
        capture_output=True, text=True)
    contracts = {str(c['id']): c['name'] for c in json.loads(r.stdout).get('contracts',[])}
    r2 = subprocess.run(['curl','-sk',
        f'https://api.smarkets.com/v3/markets/{market_id}/quotes/'],
        capture_output=True, text=True)
    raw = json.loads(r2.stdout)
    result = {}
    for cid, prices in raw.items():
        if not isinstance(prices, dict): continue
        name = contracts.get(str(cid), str(cid))
        offers = prices.get('offers', [])
        bids = prices.get('bids', [])
        def get_best(lst, fn):
            try:
                vals = [int(x[0] if isinstance(x,(list,tuple)) else x.get('price',0)) for x in lst]
                return fn(vals) / 10000 if vals else None
            except: return None
        best_offer = get_best(offers, min)
        best_bid = get_best(bids, max)
        if best_offer and best_bid:
            mid = (best_offer + best_bid) / 2; liquid = True
        elif best_offer:
            mid = best_offer * 0.945; liquid = False
        elif best_bid:
            mid = best_bid; liquid = False
        else:
            mid = None; liquid = False
        result[name] = {'offer': best_offer, 'bid': best_bid, 'mid': mid, 'liquid': liquid}
    return result

# Fetch key additional markets

}
