### CMD #123
# DESC: Compute final MEX-KOR estimates and display table
# ID: toolu_01VzrLgn5GJSmNDLJSYPi7Dx
```
python3 << 'PYEOF'
import json, math

# Final computation of all 10 MEX-KOR estimates

# Key derived lambdas
lam_mex_goals = -math.log(1 - 0.7844)   # 1.534
lam_kor_goals = -math.log(1 - 0.6452)   # 1.036

def poisson_at_least(lam, k):
    """P(X >= k) under Poisson(lam)"""
    total = 0
    for j in range(k):
        total += math.exp(-lam) * (lam**j) / math.factorial(j)
    return 1 - total

# Mexico offsides: attacking home team, λ≈1.7 (goals-weighted proxy), slight RULE8 shrink
lam_mex_off = 1.7  # attacking home side
p_mex_2plus_off = poisson_at_least(lam_mex_off, 2)  # 0.507 → shaded for RULE8
q1 = round(p_mex_2plus_off - 0.04, 2)   # slight RULE8 shrink → 0.47

# Q2: compound P(MEX first) × P(KOR 2H | MEX first)
p_mex_first = 0.5471
p_kor_2h_baseline = 0.4221
# When MEX scores first, KOR needs to chase → P(KOR 2H) elevated ~0.48
p_kor_2h_given_mex_first = 0.48
q2 = round(p_mex_first * p_kor_2h_given_mex_first, 2)  # 0.263 → round to 0.26

# Q3: Korean more corners — direct from corner handicap MEX -0.5 = 0.622
q3 = 0.38  # = 1 - 0.622

# Q4: Mexico wins — direct FTR market
q4 = 0.48  # 0.4763 rounded

# Q5: Mexico HT winning — direct HT result market
q5 = 0.35  # 0.3461

# Q6: 3+ total goals — direct OU2.5
q6 = 0.43  # 1 - 0.5683

# Q7: Korea scores in 2H — direct 2H KOR OU0.5
q7 = 0.42  # 0.4221

# Q8: 4+ cards — Cards OU3.5=0.4511 + Zwayer upward shade (~+3pp)
q8 = 0.48  # 0.4511 + Zwayer adjustment

# Q9: Berterame 1+ SOT — NOT IN SQUAD (not in 25-player ESPN roster)
# Bench: 14 confirmed players, none named Berterame
# Also absent from Smarkets player SOT and score/assist markets
q9 = 0.05  # essentially cannot play; tiny probability for data error

# Q10: Son score or assist
# Liquid goalscorer: 0.2383, Illiquid score/assist: 0.3720 (already adjusted)
# Derived P(Son assist) = (0.3720 - 0.2383)/(1 - 0.2383) = 0.175
# P(score OR assist) = 1 - (1-0.2383)(1-0.175) = 0.372
# Mild RULE15: Korea 23.3% win → -4pp shade
q10 = 0.33  # 0.372 - 0.04 RULE15 lite

# Crowd estimates (formula: crowd ≈ 0.514 + 0.61*(us - 0.5), or market-anchored for T1)
def crowd_formula(us):
    return round(0.514 + 0.61*(us - 0.5), 2)

estimates = {
    "Q1": (q1, 0.50, "Mexico 2+ offsides — Poisson λ=1.7, RULE8 shrink", "T2_realdata"),
    "Q2": (q2, 0.35, "Compound: MEX first (0.547) × KOR 2H (0.48)", "T2_compound"),
    "Q3": (q3, 0.44, "Korea more corners — direct from MEX corner handicap -0.5 = 0.622", "T1_market"),
    "Q4": (q4, 0.49, "Mexico wins — direct FTR = 0.4763", "T1_market"),
    "Q5": (q5, 0.42, "Mexico HT winning — direct HT result market = 0.3461", "T1_market"),
    "Q6": (q6, 0.47, "3+ goals — direct OU2.5 Over = 0.4317", "T1_market"),
    "Q7": (q7, 0.46, "Korea 2H goal — direct 2H KOR OU0.5 = 0.4221", "T1_market"),
    "Q8": (q8, 0.52, "4+ cards — Cards OU3.5=0.4511 + Zwayer upward 3pp", "T1_market_adjusted"),
    "Q9": (q9, 0.40, "Berterame SOT — NOT IN SQUAD (confirmed absent from 25-player ESPN roster)", "RULE9_not_in_squad"),
    "Q10": (q10, 0.42, "Son score/assist — liquid goal market 0.2383 + assist model, mild RULE15", "T1_market_RULE15"),
}

print("="*80)
print("MEX-KOR FINAL ESTIMATES")
print("="*80)
print(f"{'Q':<3} {'Our Est':>7} {'Crowd':>7} {'Delta':>7}  Method")
print("-"*80)
for q, (us, crowd, method, cat) in estimates.items():
    delta = us - crowd
    print(f"{q:<3} {us:>7.2f} {crowd:>7.2f} {delta:>+7.2f}  {method[:55]}")

print("\nλ_MEX_goals =", round(lam_mex_goals, 3))
print("λ_KOR_goals =", round(lam_kor_goals, 3))
print("P(MEX 2+off) raw =", round(p_mex_2plus_off, 3))
print("Q9 KEY EDGE: Berterame NOT IN SQUAD → 0.05 vs crowd ~0.40")
PYEOF
```

# Try likely ESPN event IDs for USA-AUS WC2026

    r = subprocess.run(['curl','-sk',
        f'https://site.api.espn.com/apis/site/v2/sports/soccer/fifa.world/summary?event={eid}'],
        capture_output=True, text=True, timeout=5)

        teams = [c['team']['displayName'] for c in comps.get('competitors',[])]
        date = comps.get('date','?')[:10]
        if any('united states' in t.lower() or 'australia' in t.lower() for t in teams):
            print(f"FOUND: event {eid}: {' vs '.join(teams)} on {date}")
            found.append(eid)
    except:
        pass
if not found:
    print("Not found in 760445-760470")

### CMD #131
# DESC: Pull confirmed lineups for USA vs Australia from ESPN
# ID: toolu_01LemTeCbLMTBhrqSy37TJJT
```
python3 << 'PYEOF'
import subprocess, json

r = subprocess.run(['curl','-sk',
    'https://site.api.espn.com/apis/site/v2/sports/soccer/fifa.world/summary?event=760442'],
    capture_output=True, text=True)
d = json.loads(r.stdout)

print("=== LINEUPS ===")
for team in d.get('rosters',[]):
    tname = team.get('team',{}).get('displayName','?')
    print(f"\n{tname}:")
    starters = [a for a in team.get('roster',[]) if a.get('starter')]
    bench = [a for a in team.get('roster',[]) if not a.get('starter')]
    print("  STARTERS:")
    for a in starters:
        name = a.get('athlete',{}).get('displayName','?')
        pos = a.get('position',{}).get('abbreviation','?')
        print(f"    {name} ({pos})")
    print(f"  BENCH ({len(bench)} players):")
    for a in bench:

### CMD #132
# DESC: Pull key Smarkets prices for USA-AUS
# ID: toolu_01S9TAhZiy695uCSQ7mHmiZU
```
python3 << 'PYEOF'
import subprocess, json

def get_prices(market_id):
    r = subprocess.run(['curl','-sk',
        f'https://api.smarkets.com/v3/markets/{market_id}/contracts/'],
        capture_output=True, text=True)
    contracts = {str(c['id']): c['name'] for c in json.loads(r.stdout).get('contracts',[])}
    r2 = subprocess.run(['curl','-sk',
        f'https://api.smarkets.com/v3/markets/{market_id}/quotes/'],
        capture_output=True, text=True)
    raw = json.loads(r2.stdout)
    result = {}
    for cid, prices in raw.items():
        if not isinstance(prices, dict): continue
        name = contracts.get(str(cid), str(cid))
        offers = prices.get('offers', [])
        bids = prices.get('bids', [])
        def get_best(lst, fn):
            try:
                vals = [int(x[0] if isinstance(x,(list,tuple)) else x.get('price',0)) for x in lst]
                return fn(vals)/10000 if vals else None
            except: return None
        best_offer = get_best(offers, min)
        best_bid = get_best(bids, max)
        if best_offer and best_bid:
            mid = (best_offer+best_bid)/2; liq=True
        elif best_offer:
            mid = best_offer*0.945; liq=False
        elif best_bid:
            mid = best_bid; liq=False
        else:
            mid = None; liq=False
        result[name] = {'mid': mid, 'liquid': liq}
    return result

markets = {
    'FTR': 139872862,
    'OU2.5': 139872899,
    'HT_result': 139872869,
    'USA_OU0.5_goals': 139872910,
    'AUS_OU0.5_goals': 139872920,
    'USA_OU1.5_goals': 139872911,
    'AUS_OU1.5_goals': 139872921,
    '2H_USA_OU0.5': 139872917,
    '2H_AUS_OU0.5': 139872927,
    '1H_USA_OU0.5': 139872914,
    '1H_AUS_OU0.5': 139872924,
    'Cards_OU3.5': 139873018,
    'Most_cards': 139872886,
    'Corner_handicap_USA-1.5': 139872981,
    'Corner_handicap_USA-0.5': 139872945,
    'Team_score_first': 139873052,
    'BTTS': 139872864,
}

for mname, mid in markets.items():
    res = get_prices(mid)
    print(f"\n{mname}:")
    for cname, p in res.items():
        if p['mid']:
            liq = "L" if p['liquid'] else "I"
            print(f"  {cname}: {p['mid']:.4f} [{liq}]")
PYEOF

import subprocess, json

def get_prices(market_id):
    r = subprocess.run(['curl','-sk',
        f'https://api.smarkets.com/v3/markets/{market_id}/contracts/'],
        capture_output=True, text=True)
    contracts = {str(c['id']): c['name'] for c in json.loads(r.stdout).get('contracts',[])}
    r2 = subprocess.run(['curl','-sk',
        f'https://api.smarkets.com/v3/markets/{market_id}/quotes/'],
        capture_output=True, text=True)
    raw = json.loads(r2.stdout)
    result = {}
    for cid, prices in raw.items():
        if not isinstance(prices, dict): continue
        name = contracts.get(str(cid), str(cid))
        offers = prices.get('offers', [])
        bids = prices.get('bids', [])
        def get_best(lst, fn):
            try:
                vals = [int(x[0] if isinstance(x,(list,tuple)) else x.get('price',0)) for x in lst]
                return fn(vals)/10000 if vals else None
            except: return None
        best_offer = get_best(offers, min)
        best_bid = get_best(bids, max)
        if best_offer and best_bid:
            mid = (best_offer+best_bid)/2; liq=True
        elif best_offer:
            mid = best_offer*0.945; liq=False
        elif best_bid:
            mid = best_bid; liq=False
        else:
            mid = None; liq=False
        result[name] = {'mid': mid, 'liquid': liq, 'offer': best_offer, 'bid': best_bid}
    return result

# Player SOT market + score or assist

        capture_output=True, text=True)
    contracts = {str(c['id']): c['name'] for c in json.loads(r.stdout).get('contracts',[])}
    r2 = subprocess.run(['curl','-sk',
        f'https://api.smarkets.com/v3/markets/{market_id}/quotes/'],
        capture_output=True, text=True)
    raw = json.loads(r2.stdout)
    result = {}
    for cid, prices in raw.items():
        if not isinstance(prices, dict): continue
        name = contracts.get(str(cid), str(cid))
        offers = prices.get('offers', [])
        bids = prices.get('bids', [])
        def get_best(lst, fn):
            try:
                vals = [int(x[0] if isinstance(x,(list,tuple)) else x.get('price',0)) for x in lst]
                return fn(vals)/10000 if vals else None
            except: return None
        best_offer = get_best(offers, min)
        best_bid = get_best(bids, max)
        if best_offer and best_bid:
            mid=(best_offer+best_bid)/2; liq=True
        elif best_offer:
            mid=best_offer*0.945; liq=False
        elif best_bid:
            mid=best_bid; liq=False
        else:
            mid=None; liq=False
        result[name] = {'mid': mid, 'liquid': liq}
    return result

# Additional markets needed for USA-AUS
extra_markets = {
    'USA_SOT_OU4.5': 143909438,
    'AUS_SOT_OU2.5': 143909484,
    'Cards_handicap_USA+0.5': 139872950,

    'USA_corner_OU4.5': 139873041,
    '2H_result': 139872868,

}
for mname, mid in extra_markets.items():
    res = get_prices(mid)
    print(f"\n{mname}:")
    for cname, p in res.items():
        if p['mid']:
            liq = "L" if p['liquid'] else "I"
            print(f"  {cname}: {p['mid']:.4f} [{liq}]")

import subprocess, json

def get_prices(market_id):
    r = subprocess.run(['curl','-sk',
        f'https://api.smarkets.com/v3/markets/{market_id}/contracts/'],
        capture_output=True, text=True)
    contracts = {str(c['id']): c['name'] for c in json.loads(r.stdout).get('contracts',[])}
    r2 = subprocess.run(['curl','-sk',
        f'https://api.smarkets.com/v3/markets/{market_id}/quotes/'],
        capture_output=True, text=True)
    raw = json.loads(r2.stdout)
    result = {}
    for cid, prices in raw.items():
        if not isinstance(prices, dict): continue
        name = contracts.get(str(cid), str(cid))
        offers = prices.get('offers', [])
        bids = prices.get('bids', [])
        def get_best(lst, fn):
            try:
                vals = [int(x[0] if isinstance(x,(list,tuple)) else x.get('price',0)) for x in lst]
                return fn(vals)/10000 if vals else None
            except: return None
        best_offer = get_best(offers, min)
        best_bid = get_best(bids, max)
        if best_offer and best_bid:
            mid=(best_offer+best_bid)/2; liq=True
        elif best_offer:
            mid=best_offer*0.945; liq=False
        elif best_bid:
            mid=best_bid; liq=False
        else:
            mid=None; liq=False
        result[name] = {'mid': mid, 'liquid': liq}
    return result

markets = {
    'BTTS_and_OU2.5': 139872892,
    'Penalty': 139872887,

    'AUS_SOT_OU1.5': 143909484,  # was 2.5 earlier, try 1.5
    'AUS_SOT_OU2.5_retry': 143909484,
}

for mname, mid in markets.items():

        print(f"\n{mname}:")

            if p['mid']:
                liq = "L" if p['liquid'] else "I"
                print(f"  {cname}: {p['mid']:.4f} [{liq}]")
    else:
        print(f"\n{mname}: no data")

### CMD #146
# DESC: Compute all 10 USA-AUS estimates with notes
# ID: toolu_01LwgdUj24sC5ViMYCQj29BZ
```
python3 << 'PYEOF'
import json, math

# Key lambdas
lam_usa = -math.log(1 - 0.8406)   # 1.836 (from OU0.5)
lam_aus = -math.log(1 - 0.6049)   # 0.929

def poisson_at_least(lam, k):
    total = sum(math.exp(-lam) * (lam**j) / math.factorial(j) for j in range(k))
    return 1 - total

# AUS offsides Poisson
p_aus_off = poisson_at_least(0.45, 2)  # conservative λ=0.45 for defensive underdog

# AUS more corners Skellam
lam_usa_cor = 5.5  # from USA corner OU4.5 Over=0.6314
lam_aus_cor = 3.0  # from AUS corner OU3.5 Over=0.3802

# Normal approx to Skellam for P(AUS > USA corners)
mean_diff = lam_aus_cor - lam_usa_cor  # -2.5
var = lam_aus_cor + lam_usa_cor        # 8.5
from math import erf, sqrt
def normal_cdf(x): return 0.5 * (1 + erf(x / sqrt(2)))
p_aus_more_corners = normal_cdf(mean_diff / sqrt(var))

# USA more 2H SOT Skellam
lam_usa_sot_2h = 2.5   # λ_full≈5.0 × 0.5
lam_aus_sot_2h = 1.25  # λ_full≈2.5 × 0.5
mean_sot = lam_usa_sot_2h - lam_aus_sot_2h  # 1.25
var_sot = lam_usa_sot_2h + lam_aus_sot_2h   # 3.75
p_usa_more_sot_raw = normal_cdf(mean_sot / sqrt(var_sot))
p_usa_more_sot_shrunk = p_usa_more_sot_raw * 0.82 + 0.5 * 0.18  # RULE12 moderate shrink

estimates = {
    "Q1": (0.40, 0.49, "USA more fouls — card proxy (Most Cards AUS=50%, USA=24%), RULE12 caution"),
    "Q2": (0.15, 0.37, "AUS 2+ offsides — 9/9 NO family, AUS 17.7% win prob, defensive underdog"),
    "Q3": (0.47, 0.49, "USA more 2H goals — direct 2H result market USA=0.4768"),
    "Q4": (0.62, 0.57, "USA more 2H SOT — Skellam λ(2.5 vs 1.25)=0.74, RULE12 shrink, RULE14 floor 0.47"),
    "Q5": (0.20, 0.36, "AUS more corners — Skellam λ(3.0 vs 5.5)=0.20, corner OU markets"),
    "Q6": (0.39, 0.46, "BTTS + 3+ goals — DIRECT Smarkets market = 0.3863"),
    "Q7": (0.59, 0.57, "USA wins — RULE1 avg(crowd=0.573, market=0.597)=0.585→0.59"),
    "Q8": (0.40, 0.48, "4+ cards — direct OU3.5 market = 0.3989, referee unknown"),
    "Q9": (0.73, 0.62, "Balogun 1+ SOT — DIRECT LIQUID market = 0.7281, USA expected winner"),
    "Q10": (0.15, 0.38, "McGree 1+ SOT — NOT in Smarkets OR ESPN data; likely absent/bench"),
}

print("="*80)
print("USA-AUS PRELIMINARY ESTIMATES (pre-lineup confirmation)")
print("="*80)
print(f"{'Q':<3} {'Us':>6} {'Crowd':>6} {'Delta':>7}  Method")
print("-"*80)
for q, (us, crowd, method) in estimates.items():
    print(f"{q:<3} {us:>6.2f} {crowd:>6.2f} {us-crowd:>+7.2f}  {method[:60]}")

print(f"\nλ_USA = {lam_usa:.3f}, λ_AUS = {lam_aus:.3f}")
print(f"P(AUS 2+ offsides | λ=0.45) = {p_aus_off:.3f}")
print(f"P(AUS more corners | Skellam) = {p_aus_more_corners:.3f}")
print(f"P(USA more 2H SOT | Skellam raw) = {p_usa_more_sot_raw:.3f} → shrunk = {p_usa_more_sot_shrunk:.3f}")

print("\n⚠️  KEY FLAGS:")
print("  Q1  RISK: No direct fouls market, RULE10 danger. Card proxy only.")
print("  Q2  EDGE: 2+ offsides family 9/9 NO. Biggest expected edge vs crowd.")
print("  Q5  EDGE: Corner markets heavily favor USA. AUS barely gets corners.")
print("  Q9  EDGE: Liquid market = 0.73. Crowd likely at 0.62. USA winner's striker.")
print("  Q10 EDGE: McGree absent from Smarkets + ESPN. Crowd ~0.38. CONFIRM LINEUP.")

    capture_output=True, text=True)

for team in d.get('rosters',[]):

    starters = [a for a in team.get('roster',[]) if a.get('starter')]
    bench = [a for a in team.get('roster',[]) if not a.get('starter')]
    print(f"\n{tname}: {len(starters)} starters, {len(bench)} bench")

    for a in bench[:5]:

header = d.get('header',{}).get('competitions',[{}])[0]

        if not isinstance(prices, dict): continue

                vals = [int(x[0] if isinstance(x,(list,tuple)) else x.get('price',0)) for x in lst]
                return fn(vals)/10000 if vals else None
            except: return None

                                 'second-half-scotland','second-half-morocco',
                                 'first-half-scotland','first-half-morocco',

### CMD #150
# DESC: Pull player SOT and goalscorer markets for Scotland vs Morocco
# ID: toolu_01AbQaiUQQEAev1a972JMEz1
```
python3 << 'PYEOF'
import subprocess, json

# Get player markets for Scotland-Morocco
def get_prices(market_id):
    r = subprocess.run(['curl','-sk',
        f'https://api.smarkets.com/v3/markets/{market_id}/contracts/'],
        capture_output=True, text=True)
    contracts = {str(c['id']): c['name'] for c in json.loads(r.stdout).get('contracts',[])}
    r2 = subprocess.run(['curl','-sk',
        f'https://api.smarkets.com/v3/markets/{market_id}/quotes/'],
        capture_output=True, text=True)
    raw = json.loads(r2.stdout)
    result = {}
    for cid, prices in raw.items():
        if not isinstance(prices, dict): continue
        name = contracts.get(str(cid), str(cid))
        offers = prices.get('offers', [])
        bids = prices.get('bids', [])
        def get_best(lst, fn):
            try:
                vals = [int(x[0] if isinstance(x,(list,tuple)) else x.get('price',0)) for x in lst]
                return fn(vals)/10000 if vals else None
            except: return None
        best_offer = get_best(offers, min)
        best_bid = get_best(bids, max)
        if best_offer and best_bid:
            mid=(best_offer+best_bid)/2; liq=True
        elif best_offer:
            mid=best_offer*0.945; liq=False
        elif best_bid:
            mid=best_bid; liq=False
        else:
            mid=None; liq=False
        result[name] = {'mid': mid, 'liquid': liq}
    return result

r = subprocess.run(['curl','-sk',
    'https://api.smarkets.com/v3/events/45067767/markets/'],
    capture_output=True, text=True)
all_markets = json.loads(r.stdout).get('markets',[])

for m in all_markets:
    slug = m.get('slug','')
    if slug in ['player-shots-target-over-0.5','player-score-or-assist','anytime-goalscorer']:
        res = get_prices(m['id'])
        print(f"\n{m['name']}:")
        for cname, p in res.items():
            if p['mid'] and p['mid'] > 0.12:
                print(f"  {cname}: {p['mid']:.4f} [{'L' if p['liquid'] else 'I'}]")
PYEOF
```

### CMD #151
# DESC: Fetch FTR, cards, corners, and 2H team goal markets for Scotland-Morocco
# ID: toolu_015kgUkUe5kouUNtdPbu57Py
```
python3 << 'PYEOF'
import subprocess, json

def get_prices(mid):
    r = subprocess.run(['curl','-sk', f'https://api.smarkets.com/v3/markets/{mid}/contracts/'], capture_output=True, text=True)
    contracts = {str(c['id']): c['name'] for c in json.loads(r.stdout).get('contracts',[])}
    r2 = subprocess.run(['curl','-sk', f'https://api.smarkets.com/v3/markets/{mid}/quotes/'], capture_output=True, text=True)
    raw = json.loads(r2.stdout)
    result = {}
    for cid, prices in raw.items():
        if not isinstance(prices, dict): continue
        name = contracts.get(str(cid), str(cid))
        offers = prices.get('offers', [])
        bids = prices.get('bids', [])
        def gb(lst, fn):
            try: return fn([int(x[0] if isinstance(x,(list,tuple)) else x.get('price',0)) for x in lst])/10000
            except: return None
        bo, bb = gb(offers, min), gb(bids, max)
        if bo and bb: mid_p=(bo+bb)/2; liq=True
        elif bo: mid_p=bo*0.945; liq=False
        elif bb: mid_p=bb; liq=False
        else: mid_p=None; liq=False
        result[name] = {'mid': mid_p, 'liquid': liq}
    return result

# Find and fetch FTR, 2H MAR OU0.5, cards markets, corner markets
r = subprocess.run(['curl','-sk', 'https://api.smarkets.com/v3/events/45067767/markets/'], capture_output=True, text=True)
all_markets = json.loads(r.stdout).get('markets',[])

target_slugs = {
    'full-time-result': 'FTR',
    'cards-over-under-2.5': 'Cards_OU2.5',
    'cards-over-under-3.5': 'Cards_OU3.5',
    'cards-winner': 'Most_cards',
    'scotland-over-under-1.5-cards': 'SCO_cards_OU1.5',
    'morocco-over-under-1.5-cards': 'MAR_cards_OU1.5',
    'corners-winner': 'Most_corners',
    'corners-handicap-scotland-plus-0.5': 'Corner_SCO+0.5',
    'corners-handicap-scotland-plus-1.5': 'Corner_SCO+1.5',
    'morocco-over-under-4.5-corners': 'MAR_corner_OU4.5',
    'scotland-over-under-3.5-corners': 'SCO_corner_OU3.5',
    'second-half-morocco-over-under-0.5': '2H_MAR_OU0.5',
    'second-half-scotland-over-under-0.5': '2H_SCO_OU0.5',
    'team-to-score-first-goal': 'Team_score_first',
    'morocco-over-under-0.5': 'MAR_OU0.5',
    'scotland-over-under-0.5': 'SCO_OU0.5',
}

for m in all_markets:
    slug = m.get('slug','')
    label = target_slugs.get(slug)
    if label:
        res = get_prices(m['id'])
        if any(p['mid'] for p in res.values()):
            print(f"\n{label}:")
            for cname, p in res.items():
                if p['mid']: print(f"  {cname}: {p['mid']:.4f} [{'L' if p['liquid'] else 'I'}]")
PYEOF

import json, math

# Key lambdas
lam_mar = -math.log(1-0.8131)   # 1.676
lam_sco = -math.log(1-0.5156)   # 0.725

def poisson_at_least(lam, k):
    return 1 - sum(math.exp(-lam)*(lam**j)/math.factorial(j) for j in range(k))

from math import erf, sqrt
def ncdf(x): return 0.5*(1+erf(x/sqrt(2)))

# Q2: Morocco 2+ offsides (attacking heavy favorite)
lam_mar_off = 1.3  # high attacking intent but disciplined
p_mar_2plus_off = poisson_at_least(lam_mar_off, 2)

# Q6: Scotland 2+ offsides (underdog but λ_goals=0.725, not pure defensive)
lam_sco_off = 0.8
p_sco_2plus_off = poisson_at_least(lam_sco_off, 2)

# Q5: Scotland more 2H SOT (Skellam)
lam_sco_sot_2h, lam_mar_sot_2h = 1.25, 2.25
mean_diff = lam_sco_sot_2h - lam_mar_sot_2h
p_sco_more_sot_raw = ncdf(mean_diff/sqrt(lam_sco_sot_2h+lam_mar_sot_2h))

estimates = {
    "Q1":  (0.33, 0.46, "Morocco more fouls — Most cards SCO 46% vs MAR 30%. Scotland fouls more as defender. Card proxy = RULE12-lite."),
    "Q2":  (0.40, 0.50, "Morocco 2+ offsides — attacking favorite, high line, λ_off=1.3 → P(2+)=0.37. NOT 9/9 NO family (Morocco is attacker)."),
    "Q3":  (0.50, 0.56, "Morocco 1+ card in 2H — λ_MAR_cards ≈ 1.4 full, 2H split λ=0.70 → P(≥1)=0.50. Cards OU3.5 Over=0.53 confirms physical match."),
    "Q4":  (0.29, 0.38, "BTTS + 3+ goals — DIRECT Smarkets market = 0.2904. LEAN UNDER (OU2.5 Under 0.587)."),
    "Q5":  (0.32, 0.42, "Scotland more 2H SOT — Skellam λ(1.25 vs 2.25) raw=0.30. RULE12 shrink → 0.32. RULE14: must be ≥ P(SCO more 2H goals)=0.15 ✓"),
    "Q6":  (0.22, 0.37, "Scotland 2+ offsides — 2+ offsides family partial apply. λ_SCO=0.725 means SCO attacks, but underdog. λ_off=0.8 → P(2+)=0.19, floor at 0.22."),
    "Q7":  (0.16, 0.22, "Scotland wins — heavy underdog. RULE1: avg(crowd~0.22, market~0.13)=0.17 → 0.16."),

print("="*80)

python3 -c "
import json
# Find the bash tool_use lines
with open('/Users/aki/.claude/projects/-Users-aki-Desktop-QK-Rstudio/6b5abc7c-fac2-48c2-bee1-2d489abc1fb2.jsonl') as f:
    for i, line in enumerate(f):

        t = obj.get('type')
        if t == 'assistant':
            msg = obj.get('message', {})
            content = msg.get('content', [])
            for block in content:

### CMD #158
# DESC: Extract all bash commands and outputs from session JSONL files
# ID: toolu_01DevSe4WqCZsrm7hjauCuVU
```
python3 << 'PYEOF'
import json, os, sys
from datetime import datetime

# Sessions to extract, with labels (date, match context)
sessions = [
    ("e61c5bc4-d530-4a2b-80eb-28e30a2db767.jsonl", "2026-06-14", "GER-CUR_BRA-MAR_JPN-NED_CIV-ECU_BEL-EGY_SAU-URU_SWE-TUN"),
    ("c0cf9c89-eacd-439e-a64a-0aacf6530444.jsonl", "2026-06-18", "GHA-PAN_UZB-COL_ENG-CRO_SUI-BIH_CAN-QAT"),
    ("aaeca6c6-5a77-4b8c-a583-b328a3768701.jsonl", "2026-06-19", "MEX-KOR_early"),
    ("6b5abc7c-fac2-48c2-bee1-2d489abc1fb2.jsonl", "2026-06-19", "MEX-KOR_USA-AUS_SCO-MAR"),
]

base_dir = "/Users/aki/.claude/projects/-Users-aki-Desktop-QK-Rstudio"
out_dir = "/Users/aki/Desktop/QK Rstudio/sportspredict_research/bash_logs"

for fname, date, label in sessions:
    fpath = os.path.join(base_dir, fname)
    if not os.path.exists(fpath):
        print(f"MISSING: {fname}")
        continue
    
    fsize = os.path.getsize(fpath) / 1e6
    print(f"Processing {fname} ({fsize:.1f}MB)...", flush=True)
    
    # Pass 1: collect all tool_use Bash blocks → {tool_use_id: {cmd, desc}}
    tool_uses = {}
    # Pass 1.5: collect all tool_result blocks → {tool_use_id: output}
    tool_results = {}
    # Track order
    order = []
    
    with open(fpath) as f:
        for line in f:
            try:
                obj = json.loads(line)
            except:
                continue
            
            t = obj.get('type')
            
            if t == 'assistant':
                msg = obj.get('message', {})
                content = msg.get('content', [])
                for block in content:
                    if isinstance(block, dict) and block.get('type') == 'tool_use' and block.get('name') == 'Bash':
                        tid = block.get('id', '')
                        inp = block.get('input', {})
                        tool_uses[tid] = {
                            'cmd': inp.get('command', ''),
                            'desc': inp.get('description', ''),
                        }
                        order.append(tid)
            
            elif t == 'user':
                msg = obj.get('message', {})
                content = msg.get('content', [])
                for block in content:
                    if isinstance(block, dict) and block.get('type') == 'tool_result':
                        tid = block.get('tool_use_id', '')
                        raw = block.get('content', '')
                        if isinstance(raw, list):
                            # list of {type, text} blocks
                            parts = []
                            for item in raw:
                                if isinstance(item, dict):
                                    parts.append(item.get('text', str(item)))
                                else:
                                    parts.append(str(item))
                            raw = '\n'.join(parts)
                        tool_results[tid] = str(raw)
    
    # Write output
    out_fname = f"{date}_{label}_bash_log.txt"
    out_path = os.path.join(out_dir, out_fname)
    
    bash_count = 0
    with open(out_path, 'w') as out:
        out.write(f"# Bash Command Log\n")
        out.write(f"# Session: {fname}\n")
        out.write(f"# Date: {date}\n")
        out.write(f"# Matches: {label}\n")
        out.write(f"# Extracted: {datetime.now().isoformat()}\n")
        out.write(f"# Total bash commands: {len(tool_uses)}\n")
        out.write("=" * 80 + "\n\n")
        
        for tid in order:
            if tid not in tool_uses:
                continue
            info = tool_uses[tid]
            bash_count += 1
            
            out.write(f"### CMD #{bash_count}\n")
            if info['desc']:
                out.write(f"# DESC: {info['desc']}\n")
            out.write(f"# ID: {tid}\n")
            out.write("```\n")
            out.write(info['cmd'])
            out.write("\n```\n\n")
            
            out.write("### OUT\n")
            result = tool_results.get(tid, '[no output recorded]')
            # Truncate very long outputs
            lines = result.split('\n')
            if len(lines) > 150:
                shown = lines[:100] + [f'\n... [TRUNCATED: {len(lines)-120} lines omitted] ...\n'] + lines[-20:]
                result = '\n'.join(shown)
            out.write(result)
            out.write("\n" + "-" * 60 + "\n\n")
    
    print(f"  → Wrote {bash_count} commands to {out_fname}")

print("\nDone.")
PYEOF
```

[no output recorded]
